[\[1b.1\]{D2174}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_ma hA yak+Sha se nA pa ta ye nI lAm+ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni ma hA ga na bi d+hiH/_bod skad du/_gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi sbyor ka chen po'i cho ga_/_
[\[1b.2\]]bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gos sngon po can la phyag 'tshal lo/_/dus gsum bde gshegs thams cad kyis/_/rig sngags gsang sngags bdag po ru/_/dbang bskur 'byung po tshar gcod pa/_/gsang sngags
[\[1b.3\]]sdud mdzad khyod phyag 'tshal/_/bcom ldan phyag na rdo rje yi/_/rgyud rnams ma lus kun dang ni/_/rnal 'byor pha rgyud ma rgyud kyi/_/rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud dang ni/_/rnal 'byor rgyud dang spyod pa'i rgyud/_/rgyud rnams
[\[1b.4\]]kun dang mi 'gal phyir/_/man ngag cung zad dran pa 'di/_/blo dman bsgrub pa'i don du ni/_/rnal 'byor cha rkyen bstan par bya/_/sbyor ba'i rim pa dpag med kyang /_/sgrub pa po yi don slad du/_/dgos
[\[1b.5\]]pa bsdus pa bstan pa 'di/_/sgrub po slob dpon dang bral na/_/sbyor ba 'di rnams bstan par gsungs/_/de la sbyor ba rim bzhin bstan/_/dang po tshogs gnyis rdzogs bya'i phyir/_/bdag nyid skad
[\[2a\]]
[\[2a.1\]]cig lhar sprul la/_/snying gar zla ba'i maN+Dal bsam/_/hUM gi 'od zer 'phros pa las/_/sgrib pa sbyangs nas phyi nang gsal/_/mdun du zla ba'i gzugs brnyan dang /_/pad+ma'i gzugs brnyan gsum mam
[\[2a.2\]]gcig_/la la gzhal yas sprul par 'dod/_/de ru dkyil 'khor bsam pa dang /_/bsod nams don phyir spyan drangs bstim/_/bla ma sbyang sogs byas nas kyang /_/gzhan sogs man ngag bzhin du bya/_/phyag 'tshal phyi
[\[2a.3\]]nang gsang bas mchod/_/mtshams med mi dge sdom nyams nas/_/rtsa ba'i dam tshig nyams pa kun/_/sgyu ma'i sems kyis bshags par bya/_/dge ba kun la rjes yi rang /_/chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar bskul/_/
[\[2a.4\]]mya ngan mi 'da' gsol ba 'debs/_/rdo rje can la skyabs su mchi/_/rdo rje rnams la lus 'bul lo/_/bsod nams ci bsags thams cad kun/_/byang chub chen por bsngo bar bya/_/tshad med bzhi yang bsgom par bya/_/de nas
[\[2a.5\]]phyi nang snod bcud kun/_/stong pa nyid du bsgom par bya/_/de nas nam mkha'i chos 'byung la/_/yi ge cho 'phrul 'phros pa las/_/'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor rim bzhin bskyed/_/de yi steng du ri rab bskyed/_/de steng rdo rje
[\[2b\]]
[\[2b.1\]]rgya gram la/_/'khor lo rtsibs bcu 'bar bas mtshan/_/zla ba'i steng du gnod mdzes sprul/_/yi ge hUM gi 'phro 'du las/_/khro bo bcu sprul hUM bzhi yi/_/gsang sngags bzlas nas bka' bsgo bya/_/khro bo sprul pas bgegs rnams bkug_/yang sgo sku gsung thugs kyi ni/_/phur bu'i
[\[2b.2\]]sngags brjod tho bas brdung /_/bsregs nas nam mkha' nyid du 'gyur/_/de nas hUM gi 'phro 'du yis/_/rdo rje gur dang ra bar 'gyur/_/yi ge b+h+rUM gyi 'phro 'du las/_/gnod mdzes 'od du zhu nas kyang /_/gzhal yas khang ni mdzes par gyur/_/de steng pad+ma 'dab brgyad gdan/_/rang
[\[2b.3\]]gi sems kyi cho 'phrul las/_/zla ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po la/_/yi ge A lis mtshan par bya/_/nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen po la/_/yi ge kA lis mtshan par bya/_/hUM las rdo rje de nyid mtshan/_/byin rlabs bsdus nas 'od du zhu/_/de las sku ni bskyed par bya/_/pad+ma dbus kyi lte ba
[\[2b.4\]]la/_/bcom ldan rdo rje gos sngon can/_/shar gyi pad+ma'i 'dab ma la/_/khro bo rnam par rgyal ba bskyed/_/lho yi pad+ma'i 'dab ma la/_/bcom ldan mgon po nag po bskyed/_/nub kyi pad+ma'i 'dab ma la/_/lus ngan rgyal po bskyed par bya/_/byang gi pad+ma'i 'dab ma la/_/bdud rtsi 'khyil pa
[\[2b.5\]]bskyed par bya/_/byang shar du ni gnod sbyin bskyed/_/shar lho ru ni ro langs ma/_/lho nub rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma/_/nub byang du ni 'jigs byed ma/_/mtshams rnams su ni lha mo bzhi/_/'od skyed ma dang yid 'phrog ma/_/kun bzang ma dang glu sgra ma/_/shar gyi sgo ru srog gcod ma/_/lho yi sgo ru
[\[2b.6\]]dbugs rngub ma/_/nub kyi phyogs su khrag 'thung ma/_/byang gi phyogs su sha za ma/_/de ltar dkyil 'khor bskyed nas kyang /_/yi ge hUM gi 'od zer dang /_/sngags dang phyag rgya'i tshigs bcad sgras/_/rang bzhin dkyil 'khor spyan drangs la/_/mchod bstod byas nas dam tshig la/_/
[\[2b.7\]]byin rlabs bstims te dbang bskur ro/_/de lta'i dkyil 'khor chen po la/_/thun bzhi thun brgyad par dag tu/_/bsgoms nas brtan par gyur pas na/_/las rnams gzhan nam rdzogs rim la/_/gzhug par bya ba kho na yin/_/'khor lo chen po'i sbyor ka ste dang po'o//_//bcom
[\[3a\]]
[\[3a.1\]]ldan rdo rje bsnams la phyag 'tshal lo/_/dkyil 'khor chen po mi nus pas/_/lha rnams so so kun la yang /_/rgyan gcig pa la sbyor ba bstan/_/dang po gtso bo'i sbyor ba ni/_/bdag nyid skad cig lhar sprul la/_/yi ge hUM gi man ngag sogs/_/rim pa bzhin du shes
[\[3a.2\]]par bya/_/phyag 'tshal mchod cing bshags pa dang /_/rjes su yi rang bskul ba dang /_/gsol ba gdab cing skyabs su gsol/_/lus 'bul dge rtsa bsngo bar bya/_/tshad med bzhi bsgom stong nyid bsgom/_/stong pa'i ngang las yi ge hUM/_/de las phyag mtshan rdo rjer gyur/_/de nyid las
[\[3a.3\]]ni sku bskyed do/_/sku mdog sngon po zhal gcig pa/_/mche ba gtsigs mdzad spyan mig bzlog_/phyag g.yas rdo rje bsnams mdzad nas/_/phyag g.yon nam mkha' lding ni bsnams/_/g.yon brkyang g.yas bskum klu la shis/_/g.yas pa rdo rje bsnams mdzad nas/_/g.yon pa rtse
[\[3a.4\]]gsum bsnams pa ni/_/gshin rje dag la shis par bstan/_/g.yas pa rdo rje gsor nas ni/_/g.yon pa dril bu bsgrags pa ni/_/gnod sbyin drag la shis par bstan/_/ye shes dkyil 'khor spyan drangs bstims/_/byin rlabs dbang bskur byas nas kyang /_/thun mtshams bzhir
[\[3a.5\]]ni brtan par bsgom/_/gtso bo'i sbyor ka ste gnyis pa'o//_//bcom ldan 'das rnam par rgyal ba la phyag 'tshal lo/_/skad cig lhar sprul thugs ka ru/_/nyi ma'i steng du hUM sogs rdzogs/_/phyag 'tshal mchod cing bshags par bya/_/rjes su yi rang la sogs bya/_/stong pa nyid du
[\[3a.6\]]bsgoms nas kyang /_/stong pa'i ngang las cho 'phrul du/_/rdo rje pad+ma'i nyi zla'i steng /_/de steng hUM las rdo rjer gyur/_/rdo rje las ni sku bskyed do/_/khro chen khams gsum rnam rgyal ni/_/sku mdog dmar po dbu gsum pa/_/phyag drug dang po rdo rje'o/_/g.yon gyi dang po dgra sta'o/_/bar ma
[\[3a.7\]]gnyis kyis 'ching byed pa/_/gung mo mthe bong ngos btud nas/_/gzhan rnams yongs su brkyang ba yin/_/de nyid snying gar bzung nas ni/_/de 'og g.yas pas zhags pa bsnams/_/g.yon pa ral gri bsnams pa'o/_/ye shes spyan drangs bstims nas kyang /_/byin rlabs
[\[3b\]]
[\[3b.1\]]dbang bskur byas nas ni/_/thun mtshams bzhi ru brtan par bsgoms/_/snying ga'i man ngag gsal nas kyang /_/lce ni rdo rjer byin gyis brlabs/_/bzlas brjod 'phros 'dus bsnyen pa bya/_/dus grangs mtshan ma thim pa dang /_/bsgrub pa gang 'dod brtsam par bya'o/_/rnam par rgyal
[\[3b.2\]]ba'i sbyor ka ste gsum pa'o//_//bcom ldan 'das dpal mgon po nag po la phyag 'tshal lo/_/skad cig lha ru sprul nas kyang /_/hUM gi man ngag rdzogs pa yis/_/phyag 'tshal mchod pa la sogs bya/_/stong pa nyid kyi ngang nyid las/_/rin chen gdan sogs rdzogs byas la/_/
[\[3b.3\]]yi ge hUM las be con gyur/_/de nyid las ni sku rdzogs gyur/_/dpal ldan mgon po nag po ni/_/sku mdog nag po dud sprin 'dra/_/zhal gcig pa la phyag gnyis pa/_/g.yas pa tsan+dan bing chen bsnams/_/g.yon pa zhags pa bsnams pa'o/_/zhabs ni brkyang bskum
[\[3b.4\]]tshul du bzhugs/_/ye shes mgon po spyan drangs bstim/_/byin rlabs dbang bskur la sogs bya/_/de ltar bstan nas bzlas brjod bya/_/mgon po mdun du spyan drangs nas/_/bzlas brjod la sogs rdzogs byas la/_/de nas sgrub pa brtsam par bya/_/mgon po las kyi
[\[3b.5\]]sbyor ka ste bzhi pa'o//_//lus ngan gsung mchog sprul la phyag 'tshal lo/_/skad cig lhar sprul hUM gis ni/_/spyan drangs la sogs rdzogs byas la/_/phyag 'tshal mchod pa la sogs bya/_/stong pa'i ngang las pad sogs gdan/_/yi ge hUM las mchod rten gyur/_/de nyid las ni sku
[\[3b.6\]]bskyed do/_/lus ngan sku mdog ljang gu'o/_/zhal gcig phyag g.yas mchod rten bsnams/_/g.yon pa le'u le bsnams pa'o/_/ye shes spyan drangs bstims nas ni/_/byin gyis brlab cing dbang bskur ro/_/bzlas brjod bsnyen pa rdzogs nas ni/_/de nas sgrub pa brtsam par bya'o/_/
[\[3b.7\]]lus ngan po'i sbyor ka ste lnga pa'o//_//khro chen bdud rtsi 'khyil la phyag 'tshal lo/_/skad cig lhar sprul hUM gis ni/_/sbyor ba la sogs rdzogs par bya/_/de nas phyag 'tshal mchod sogs bya/_/stong pa'i ngang las rdo rje'i gdan/_/de steng hUM las rdo rje'o/_/de nyid las ni sku
[\[4a\]]
[\[4a.1\]]rdzogs gyur/_/khro chen bdud rtsi 'khyil pa sku sngon po/_/zhal gcig phyag gnyis brang du bsnol/_/zhabs gnyis brkyang bskum tshul du bzhugs/_/ye shes dkyil 'khor spyan drangs bstim/_/byin gyis brlab cing dbang bskur ro/_/bsnyen pa la sogs
[\[4a.2\]]rdzogs nas ni/_/de nas bsgrub pa brtsam par bya'o/_/bdud rtsi 'khyil pa'i sbyor ka ste drug pa'o//_//mkha' 'gro ma rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/_/gnod sbyin mkha' 'gro la sogs kyang /_/sprul pa dang ni rang rgyud kyi/_/man ngag rnams ni shes par bya/_/mdun du sprul dang
[\[4a.3\]]bskyed pa ni/_/gtso bo'i dbang du bya ba dang /_/so so rang rang dbang du'o/_/de rnams cho ga la sogs kyang /_/man ngag bzhin du shes par bya'o/_/gnod sbyin kha dog dmar nag la/_/zhal gcig pa la phyag gnyis pa/_/g.yas g.yon gri gug cang te'u bsnams/_/ro langs ma ni sngo skya
[\[4a.4\]]ste/_/zhal gcig pa la phyag gnyis pa/_/rdo rje lcags sgrog bzung nas ni/_/gung mo srin lag la sogs gsum po rnams/_/dam por bkug pas yongs su bsdams/_/mtheb mdzub bzhi rnams rab brkyang ste/_/spyi bor nges par bsnol nas bsdams/_/rdo rje mkha' 'gro
[\[4a.5\]]mdog ser skya/_/phyag gnyis spyi bor sbyar nas su/_/me lce'i phreng ba yongs su 'dzin/_/'jigs byed mdog ni sngo nag la/_/zhal gsum phyag drug zhabs gnyis pa/_/g.yas kyi dang po glang po bsnams/_/g.yon pa glang po'i pags pa bsnams/_/de 'og g.yas pa rdo
[\[4a.6\]]rje bsnams/_/g.yon pa dgra sta bsnams pa'o/_/de 'og g.yas pa lcags kyu bsnams/_/g.yon pa mi mgo rlon pa bsnams/_/gnod sbyin mkha' 'gro de rnams kyang /_/gtso bo gos sngon la bskor lhan ne'i tshul/_/dkyil 'khor tshul gyis bsgom thabs dang /_/yang na so so
[\[4a.7\]]re re dang /_/rje khol tshul du gnas nas kyang /_/las rnams kun la mngags pa dang /_/yang na sbyor thabs tshul gnas nas/_/gsang mchod 'bul zhing phyag rgya bsgrub/_/gnod sbyin mkha' 'gro ma'i sbyor ka steng bdun pa'o//_//rdo rje lha mo rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/_/
[\[4b\]]
[\[4b.1\]]lha mo 'di rnams cho ga yang /_/mkha' 'gro bzhin du 'dir shes bya/_/'od skyed ma zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog dkar mo'o/_/phyag gnyis me tog bsnams pa'o/_/yid 'phrog ma zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/_/sku mdog ser mo mdzes pa'i tshul/_/phyag gnyis dri
[\[4b.2\]]yi spos phor bsnams/_/kun bzang ma zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/_/sku mdog dmar mo mdzes pa'i tshul/_/phyag gnyis zhal zas ro brgya ldan pa bsnams/_/glu sgra can ni zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/_/sku mdog sngon mo mdzes pa'i tshul/_/phyag gnyis sgra snyan gar gyis
[\[4b.3\]]rol/_/lha mo 'di rnams kun la yang /_/dkyil 'khor las dang mchod pa'i tshul/_/gsum pa'i man ngag shes mod kyang /_/khyad par mchod pa'i tshul du bstan/_/mchod pa'i lha mo'i sbyor ka ste brgyad pa'o//_//sgo ma bzhi la phyag 'tshal lo/_/sgo ma'i cho ga la sogs kyang /_/
[\[4b.4\]]gong gi cho ga sbyor shes bya'o/_/srog gcod zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/_/sku mdog mthing ga 'jigs pa'i tshul/_/phyag gnyis tho ba zhags pa bsnams/_/dbugs rngub ma zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/_/sku mdog ser mo 'jigs pa'i tshul/_/phyag gnyis hom gzar
[\[4b.5\]]zhags pa bsnams/_/khrag 'thung ma zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/_/sku mdog dmar mo 'jigs pa'i gzugs/_/phyag gnyis gri gug zhags pa bsnams/_/sha za ma zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/_/sku mdog sngon po 'jigs pa'i tshul/_/phyag gnyis rnon po zhags pa bsnams/_/
[\[4b.6\]]khro mo 'di rnams spyad tshul yang /_/dkyil 'khor las sbyor ba'i tshul/_/khyad par gsad pa'i las la shis/_/sgo ma bzhi'i sbyor ka ste dgu pa'o//_//bcom ldan 'das rdo rje bsnams pa la phyag 'tshal lo/_/rnal 'byor blo rnams rim pa yis/_/bsdus rgyas rim pa bstan
[\[4b.7\]]par bya/_/pad+ma 'dab brgyad dkyil 'khor la/_/dbus dang 'dab brgyad lha dgu'o/_/phyi rim keng rus 'bar bas bskor/_/gru chad bzhi la lha mo bzhi po gnas/_/sgo rnams bzhi la sgo ma bzhi/_/'di ni rnal 'byor rgyas pa'i tshad/_/rnal 'byor bsdus la mos pa yis/_/
[\[5a\]]
[\[5a.1\]]lha ni bcu gsum bsgom par bya/_/de las kyang ni bsdus 'dod na/_/lha ni dgu po bsgom par bya/_/de las kyang ni bsdus 'dod na/_/lnga dang gsum dang gnyis dang gcig_/man ngag cho ga mthong bas bya/_/ma mthong bas ni dam tshig nyams/_/de dag thams
[\[5a.2\]]cad kun la yang /_/tshogs bsag lha bskyed mkhas pas bya/_/bsdus rgyas kyi sbyor ka ste bcu pa'o//_//bcom ldan 'das rdo rje bsnams pa la phyag 'tshal lo/_/lha rnams mchod pa'i rim pa ni/_/sha chen po las byung ba yi/_/dri mchog dud pa rgyun mi gcad/_/bde gshegs
[\[5a.3\]]shangs la phul gyur pa/_/sku gsung thugs mchog mnyes gyur cig_/sha chen bdug spos dbul ba'o/_/b+ha ga rang byung me tog 'di/_/yid 'ong nam mkha' khyab tsam du/_/bde gshegs dbu la phul ba yis/_/sku gsung thugs mchog mnyes gyur cig_/rak+ta'i me tog
[\[5a.4\]]dbul ba'o/_/tshil chen dur khrod ras las ni/_/ma rig mun sel sgron ma byung /_/bde gshegs spyan la phul gyur pas/_/sku gsung thugs mchog mnyes gyur cig_/tshil chen mar me dbul ba'o/_/mtshan dang ldan pa'i ka pA lar/_/rdo rje dri chus bkang nas su/_/bde
[\[5a.5\]]gshegs thugs la phul gyur pas/_/sku gsung thugs mchog mnyes gyur cig_/rdo rje chu yis mchod pa'o/_/mtshan dang ldan pa'i ka pA lar/_/rdo rje dri chen gtams nas su/_/bde gshegs ljags la phul gyur pas/_/sku gsung thugs mchog mnyes gyur cig_/dri chen lha
[\[5a.6\]]bshos mchod pa'o/_/sil snyan rol mo dpag med rnams/_/yid 'ong mdzes par sprul nas su/_/bde gshegs snyan la phul gyur bas/_/sku gsung thugs mchog mnyes gyur cig_/sgra dang rol mos mchod pa'o/_/rdo rje lha mo 'od skyed ma/_/rdo rje me tog bsnams nas
[\[5a.7\]]ni/_/mdzes pa'i tshul gyis mchod phul na/_/mchod pa dam pa'i tshul gyis bzhes/_/rdo rje lha mo yid 'phrog ma/_/dri yi dung phor bsnams nas su/_/gser 'od bzhad pa'i tshul gyis su/_/mchod pa dam pa 'bul gyis bzhes/_/rdo rje lha mo kun bzang ma/_/zhal zas ro mchog
[\[5b\]]
[\[5b.1\]]bsnams nas su/_/dmar mo bzhad pa'i tshul gyis ni/_/mchod pa dam pa 'bul lo bzhes/_/rdo rje lha mo glu sgra can/_/sgra snyan gar gyi rol mo yis/_/'od sngon 'phros pa'i bzhad tshul gyis/_/mchod pa dam pa 'bul lo bzhes/_/sgeg mo la sogs brgyad rnams kyang /_/
[\[5b.2\]]rgyud rnams gzhan dang mthun pas na/_/de bzhin 'dir yang dbul bar bya/_/rdo rje glu rnams mdzes pa yis/_/bstun nas lha la mchod pa 'bul/_/mchod pa'i sbyor ka ste bcu gcig pa'o//_//bcom ldan 'das rdo rje can la phyag 'tshal lo/_/lha rnams bstod pa'i rim
[\[5b.3\]]pa ni/_/bcom ldan rdo rje gos sngon can/_/sku mdog sngon po 'jigs pa'i tshul/_/rdo rje stobs kyis 'byung po 'dul/_/rdo rje bsnams la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/rnam rgyal rdo rje khro bo ni/_/dbu gsum phyag drug 'jigs pa'i gzugs/_/sku mdog 'od dmar bgegs rnams
[\[5b.4\]]bsreg_/bdud las rgyal la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/dpal ldan mgon po nag po ni/_/nag po'i zhags pa 'dzin mdzad cing /_/tsan+dan bing gis thams cad 'joms/_/mthu chen khyod la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/lus ngan po ni rgyal po'i mchog_/mchod pa'i rten gyis don rnams
[\[5b.5\]]'grub/_/ne'u le rin chen gter brtan bsnams/_/dgos 'dod skong la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/khro bo bdud rtsis bdud rnams 'joms/_/phyag rgya sdigs mdzub mdzad pa yis/_/sdang mig mi 'gyur zhe la gnon/_/'od sngon po la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/gnod sbyin khro bo
[\[5b.6\]]'jigs pa'i gzugs/_/sku mdog dmar nag 'od zer can/_/gri gug 'bar bas gcod mdzad ma/_/cang te'u sgrogs la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/ro langs ma ni mthu mo che/_/sngo skya rdo rje lcags sgrog sdom/_/phyag rgya spyi bor bsnol mdzad ma/_/ro langs ma la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/rdo rje mkha'
[\[5b.7\]]'gro dpal 'bar ma/_/dmar skya me lce phreng ba 'dzin/_/rdo rje mes ni thams cad bsreg_/rdo rje mkha' 'gro phyag 'tshal bstod/_/'jigs byed ma ni thams cad 'joms/_/sngo nag zhal gsum phyag drug pa/_/phyag mtshan drug gis 'byung po 'dul/_/'jigs byed ma la phyag
[\[6a\]]
[\[6a.1\]]'tshal bstod/_/rdo rje lha mo 'od skyed ma/_/zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog dkar/_/rdo rje me tog phyag na bsnams/_/'od skyed ma la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/rdo rje lha mo yid 'phrog ma/_/zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog ser/_/dri mchog dpag
[\[6a.2\]]med phyag na bsnams/_/yid 'phrog ma la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/rdo rje lha mo kun bzang ma/_/zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog dmar/_/zhal zas ro mchog brgya ldan bsnams/_/kun bzang ma la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/rdo rje lha mo glu sgra can/_/zhal gcig phyag
[\[6a.3\]]gnyis sku mdog sngo/_/sgra snyan gar gyi rol pas gnas/_/glu sgra can la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/rdo rje khro mo srog gcod ma/_/zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog gnag_/sgrub la gnod pa'i srog gcod ma/_/tho ba zhags pa bsnams la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/khro mo
[\[6a.4\]]rdo rje dbugs rngub ma/_/zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog ser/_/sgrub la gnod pa'i dbugs rngub ma/_/hom gzar zhags pa bsnams la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/khro mo chen mo khrag 'thung ma/_/zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog dmar/_/sgrub la gnod pa'i khrag
[\[6a.5\]]'thung ma/_/gri gug zhags pa bsnams la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/khro mo chen mo sha za ma/_/zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog sngo/_/sgrub la gnod pa'i sha za ma/_/rnon po zhags pa bsnams la phyag 'tshal bstod/_/rdo rje glu ni mdzes pa yis/_/bstod pa rnams kyis lha bstod pas/_/
[\[6a.6\]]tshogs chen dpag med sogs par 'gyur/_/bstod pa'i sbyor ka ste bcu gnyis pa'o//_//bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa la phyag 'tshal te/_/rdor dril byin brlabs mchod pa bstan/_/rdor dril rab gnas byas pa dang /_/dang po stong dang snying rje las/_/yi ge oM hUM rnam gnyis

[\[10b.1\]]don dam rang bzhin med pa la/_/kun rdzob sgyu ma lta bu'i sems/_/re dang dogs pa rnams spangs te/_/dga' dang mi dga'i sems mi bya/_/'jigs pa la sogs sems spangs te/_/maN+Dal me tog bcas phul nas/_/sbyin sreg 'khor lo la sogs bya/_/de ltar byas

[\[10b.3\]]pa tha ma'o/_/grangs kyi rab 'bring tha ma ni/_/gtso bo 'bum dang nyis 'bum dang /_/sum 'bum dag tu shes par bya/_/rnam rgyal la sogs bzhi po la/_/'bum phyed 'bum dang nyis 'bum mo/_/'khor rnams lhag ma kun la ni/_/khri dang nyi khri sum khri'o/_/yang na

[\[15a.1\]]ltar gsal nas bzlas brjod bya/_/thugs 'khor gsal dang lha mchod dang /_/sbyang dang bsdu ba'i tshul bzhin du/_/'bum gsum bsnyen pa bya ba dang /_/dus dang grangs dang mtshan ma yi/_/bsnyen pa la sogs tshad phyin nas/_/de nas 'khor rnams

[\[19a\]]
[\[19a.1\]]bkang ste thod pa gsum sgyed bzhag_/dur khrod dag gi ro shing bskul/_/khros pa'i me yis bskul bar bya/_/dur khrod ras mar bsgrub bya'i ming gzugs bri/_/steng gi thod pa bcug ste bzhag_/thod pa kha sbub thal ba phyogs su gtor/_/'dis ni nges par gsod

[\[19b\]]
[\[19b.1\]]dag la gdags/_/'khor zhing 'khrug cing myos par 'gyur/_/yang na skad cig tsam gyis 'gugs/_/oM nI lAm+bar d+ha ra ma hA ya k+Sha se nA pa ta ye badzra pA Ni ye hUM hUM phaT phaT/_de ba dat+ta mA ra ya hUM che ge mo dzaH/_zhes bya ba yi sngags kyis na/_/ji ltar 'dod pa 'di rnams 'grub/_/
[\[19b.2\]]'gugs pa la sogs pa'i 'khrul 'khor gyi sbyor ka ste nyi shu bdun pa'o//_//bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa la phyag 'tshal lo/_/lung bstan sbyor ba'i man ngag ni/_/rgyud rnams kun dang mi 'gal ba'i/_/mkha' 'gro ma yis rgyas btab la/_/rnal 'byor bla dman don du ni/_/

[\[20a\]]
[\[20a.1\]]gis/_/dngos grub bsgrub par gsungs pa yin/_/des ma byung na bzlas brjod do/_/des ma byung na gtor ma'o/_/de rnams kun la ma byung na/_/las kyi phran tshegs gzhan yang bstan/_/yang na de dag thams cad kyang /_/gcig 'dus gnyis 'dus gsum 'dus

[\[20a.5\]]kyi ni gzhung gis kyang /_/skye ba bdun las mi 'da' bas/_/ma bsgoms kyang ni sangs rgyas sa/_/zhes su rgyud las gsungs pa yin/_/skye ba bdun zhes bya ba yang /_/sngags pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yin/_/sngags dang sman la sogs pa yi/_/stobs kyis lus sems las
[\[20a.6\]]rung ba'i/_/sha dang thod pa la sogs pa/_/bsten cing zos pas dngos grub thob/_/de bas sngags mthu'i yon tan no/_/sa dang pha rol phyin pa la/_/skye ba bdun pa 'ong srid kyang /_/de lta 'ong ba shin tu dkon/_/skye ba bdun pa zhes bya'i gnas/_phal cher dur khrod chen po yi/_/

[\[20b\]]
[\[20b.1\]]skye ba bdun pa'i gang zag ni/_/mi yul gnas ni khyad par can/_/sngags spyod pa yi gnas dag tu/_/'ga' tsam 'byung ba dag kyang yod/_/skye ba gcig pa la sogs gzhan/_/de rnams gnas kyang de bzhin no/_/skye ba bdun pa'i gang zag ni/_/dad dang snying rje la sogs

[\[21a\]]
[\[21a.1\]]pa yi man ngag rnams/_/ston par byed na skye bdun sogs/_/sngags kyi dngos grub thob pa yi/_/rnal 'byor rig 'dzin byang chub sems/_/yang na dang po skyes nas ni/_/theg chen chos la mos nas kyang /_/man ngag bsgom la shin tu dga'/_/slob dpon la ni

[\[22b.6\]]bar chod mkhan/_/de ltar gnyis su ma shes na/_/dngos grub thob kyang slar la 'chor/_/de gnyis gzugs dang rtags sogs kyang /_/gong ma bzhin du ston pas na/_/de yi rim pa'ang gong bzhin bya/_/de yang brtag pa'i cho ga yang /_/zhag gsum zhag bdun rtsa gcig tu/_/

[\[23a\]]
[\[23a.1\]]gsal 'bar zhing /_/gzugs dang sgra dang dri la sogs/_/thams cad brten zhing mi 'gyur ba/_/lha yi mtshan mar shes par bya'o/_/de las bzlog pa thams cad kun/_/bdud kyi rtags su shes par bya'o/_/de la sogs pa mtha' yas mchog_/_

[\[23a.3\]]'bul mi nus/_/de la man ngag bstan mi bya/_/de la man ngag bstan pa na/_/dngos grub nyams te sdig pa 'phel/_/dam tshig nyams te mkha' 'gros gsod/_/cha rkyen la sogs bcu bdun po/_/ston pa phyag na rdo rje yis/_/sems dpa' phyag na rdo rje la/_/rna ba brgyud

[\[23a.5\]]ni/_/klu rgyal gtsug nas rnyed nas ni/_/'dam rdzab nang du stor ba bzhin/_/de bzhin man ngag rin chen 'di/_/lus ngag yid gsum dka' ba yi/_/sgo nas slob dpon la btsal nas/_/dam med rmongs pa'i lag shor na/_/dngos grub mi thob nyams par 'gyur/_/de bas

[\[23b\]]
[\[23b.1\]]dang po maN+Dal dkar po bca'/_/gnyis pa sngon po dag tu bya/_/gsum pa mthing ga dag tu bya/_/bzhi pa ser po dag tu bya/_/lnga pa dmar po dag tu bya/_/dkar rtsi dang ni ba bla dang /_/yang na rtswa sngon me tog gis/_/gnyis pa dang ni gsum pa ni/_/mtshal la sogs pa'i rigs
[\[23b.2\]]dang ni/_/gur gum la sogs rigs dag dang /_/sbyar ba'i nag po'i rigs dag gis/_/kha dog bsgyur bar bstan pa yin/_/yang na thams cad dkar dang sngo/_/de gnyis gcig gis bya ba yin/_/bsdus rgyas mkhas pas shes par bya/_/ba yi rnam pa lnga dang ni/_/bdud rtsi rnam pa lnga dag ni/_/dngos grub can
[\[23b.3\]]gyi snod du gzhag_/rin chen bum pa la sogs kyi/_/skyon spangs yon tan ldan pa yi/_/snod du thun mong khyad par rdzas/_/tsan+dan med du mi rung ngo /_/kha rgyan 'bras bu can gyis bya/_/dang por bdag nyid rnal 'byor pas/_/tha mal 'du shes spangs nas ni/_/lha yi nga rgyal ldan pa yis/_/
[\[23b.4\]]dang po bum pa byin gyis brlabs/_/bdud rtsi 'khyil pa'i sngags kyis gdab/_/oM a mr-i ta kuN+Da li hUM/_nyi shu rtsa gcig bdun du gdab/_/gong gi bkra shis snod kyi rdzas/_/bdud rtsi 'khyil pas btab nas kyang /_/dang po bum pa'i chus su bsang /_/bdud rtsi 'khyil
[\[23b.5\]]pa'i sngags kyang bzlas/_/thugs ka'i a las zla ba yi/_/dkyil 'khor chen po nyid du bsam/_/oM a tsan+d+ra maN+Dal hUM/_/bdun dang lnga dang gsum du bzlas/_/tsan+dan las kyi bum pas bsang /_/yi ge du 'phros tsan+dan phog_/de las 'phros pas maN+Dal gang /_/oM d+hUM pa s+pha
[\[23b.6\]]ra Na hUM/_zhes pas lan bdun bzlas so/_/me tog lnga dang gnyis gcig la/_/kha dog mtshan nyid shes byas la/_/yi ge paM las pad+ma ni/_/stong ldan brgyad ldan dag tu ni/_/gyur par bsams nas sngags bzlas dgram/_/oM baM pad+ma maN+Dal hUM/_zhes gong ma bzhin du

[\[24a\]]
[\[24a.1\]]nyams pa che chung go rims so/_/de nas rnal 'byor bdag nyid dang /_/dam tshig nyams pa'i rnal 'byor kun/_/khrus byas gos ni bzang po gon/_/rgyan cha la sogs mdzes par byas/_/shar ram nub tu kha bltas te/_/so so lha yi ting 'dzin bskyed/_/rdo rje

[\[30a.1\]]cho ga rnam lngas lhar bskyed pa/_/gang yang rung byas byin gyis brlab/_/gtor ma'i rdzas ni thun mong rdzas steng du/_/khyad par rdzas ni rak+ta sna tshogs dang /_/gshog pa can gyi sha sna sna chogs shis/_/byin gyis brlabs la bde gshegs mchod/_/gnyis pa mkha' 'gro ma

[\[31a\]]
[\[31a.1\]]rtse lnga sbu gu can du bsams la/_des drangs la gsol bar bsam/_bstabs pa'i sngags ni/_oM ba su ki ba liM ta khA hi zhes klu rnams kyi so so'i rtsa ba'i sngags la btags la dbul bar bya'o/_/gshegs su gsol ba'i sngags ni badzra muHzhes btags

[\[31a.7\]]tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i cho ga_/dpal rdo rje can la phyag 'tshal lo/_/tshogs chen khyad par bsags pa dang /_/dam tshig nyams pa bskang ba dang /_/sgrib sbyang mchog ni thob bya'i phyir/_/rnal 'byor lugs mthun bdag gis bshad/_/tshogs ni gnyis su shes par bya'o/_/

[\[31b.1\]]phan gdags pa dang tshar gcad pa'i/_/de yang 'khor lo bskor dang mchod pa brtsam/_/phan pa mchog dang thun mong ngo /_/dgug dang bskrad dang mnan pa dang /_/gsad pa la sogs tshar gcad pa'o/_/de sgrub rnal 'byor bstan pa ni/_/sngags pa gcig tu rtog byed dang /_/
[\[31b.2\]]dus rnams kun du rtse gcig ldan/_/rgyud rnams kyi ni snying po shes/_/de nyid bcu ni mchog tu rig_/zab cing rgya chen chos la mos/_/yid ni shin tu 'jam pa dang /_/bsnyen bkur ldan zhing 'jigs pa med/_/nga rgyal med cing gshegs la brtson/_/brda dang phyag rgya'i

[\[32a\]]
[\[32a.1\]]grub chen po 'thob/_/yon tan sbyor ba'i rim pa dang /_/sgrub po 'dod pa'i rim pa yis/_/gong gi khyad par shes par bya/_/phyi ltar ba yi rnam lngas byug_/nang ni bdud rtsi rnam lngas byug_/phyi ni mdzes pa'i rgyan rnams bris/_/nang ni dur khrod chas kyis

[\[32a.3\]]sbyang /_/las kyi sems dpa' gral la dgod/_/rgyan cha gan la go bgor gnas/_/slob dpon gyis ni byin brlabs shing /_/las kyi sems mas rtags gsum gdab/_/rang gis lhag pa'i nga rgyal bya/_/gar mas maN+Dal mchod pa rnams/_/rim par byas nas gsol ba

[\[32a.5\]]tshogs kyi dbye ba bstan pa ni/_/rtsa ba lnga las rtsa lngar gyur/_/thun mong du ni brgya bya la/_/rnal 'byor zab mo'i spyod pa yin/_/sha yi bye brag nyi shu lnga/_/btung ba'i bye brag de bzhin no/_/sman gyi bye brag nyi shu dang /_/bshos dang dkar gyi bye brag kyang /_/phyed mar byas pa'i sum cu
[\[32a.6\]]yin/_/spos kyi bye brag brgyad du bstan/_/de nas bsdus pa phyed du bstan/_/shin tu bsdus pa de yi phyed/_/de ni tshogs kyi 'khor lo'o/_/tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i mchod pa'i rim pa ni/_/bcu dang lnga dang gsum du bya/_/de yi rab 'bring sgrub pa'o/_/bsod nams che chung rim pa
[\[32a.7\]]de'o/_/tshogs de slob dpon byin gyis brlabs/_/rlung gis me sbar mtshan ldan dros/_/de nyid gsum gyi las byas la/_/bdud rtsi bab cing rdo rjes dkrugs/_/bdud rtsi'i rang bzhin 'od du zhu/_/btung ba'i byin rlabs la sogs kyang /_/man ngag bzhin du byin brlabs la/_/
[\[32b\]]
[\[32b.1\]]bdud rtsi mchod pa phyogs bkram la/_/dang po las kyi rnal 'byor gyis/_/mdun du lha bskyed spyan drangs bstim/_/dang po phyag 'tshal mchod lnga 'bul/_/de nas bdud rtsi'i mchod pa 'bul/_/de 'og lcags kyu lnga po dang /_/glu dang gar gyi mchod pa 'bul/_/hUM gi glu
[\[32b.2\]]blangs mchod pa ni/_/nyi shu yang ni bya bar gsungs/_/bstod cing rol mo'i mchod pa 'bul/_/de nas rnal 'byor rnams la mchod/_/lhag ma mkha' 'gro rnams la mchod/_/maN+Dal sngon po byas nas ni/_/bdud rtsi lnga yis chag chag gdab/_/me tog sngon po'i tshom bu bya/_/
[\[32b.3\]]sa la gnas pa'i mkha' 'gro ma/_/bskyed cing spyan drangs bstim byas la/_/byin gyis brlabs la mchod pa bya/_/lhag ma kha chus btab nas ni/_/sbyang dang spro ba bsdus byas la/_/'khor khang phyi logs maN+Dal bya/_/khrag gis byug cing me tog dgram/_/bshud glu brda
[\[32b.4\]]yis spyan drangs nas/_/rnal 'byor skra bshig thal bas byug_/rgyan chas gon la rtags rnams gdab/_/lha yi ting 'dzin gsal byas nas/_/rdo rje'i glu blangs rol mo brdung /_/mchod cing bstod nas mthol bshags bya/_/phrin las bcol la gshegs su gsol/_/
[\[32b.5\]]tshogs kyi sbyor ka'i phrin las kyis/_/rnal 'byor pa yi las rnams 'grub/_/slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa rdzogs so//_@#/_/zab ba don gyi cho ga rnams/_/rin chen lta bu'i gang zag la/_/zab phyir man ngag bkol nas bstan/_/mchog gi tshogs
[\[32b.6\]]kyi 'khor lo ni/_/thun mong cho ga thams cad ni/_/thun mong tshogs 'khor dang mthun no/_/khyad par cho ga bstan pa ni/_/rin chen phub pa dgu rim mam/_/bdun rim lnga rim sum rim ni/_/mu stegs nyan thos skye bo yis/_/skrag 'gyur log spyod spyad byed gsum/_/
[\[32b.7\]]de dag spang phyir gong bzhin bstan/_/rgyal rigs rje'u rigs bram ze'i rigs/_/bu mo mtshan dang ldan pa ni/_/mtshan rnams bcu po rdzogs pa dang /_/shes rab che dang snying rje che/_/dad pa la sogs che ba dang /_/rnal 'byor ldan pa phyag rgya mkhas/_/sbyor thabs
[\[33a\]]
[\[33a.1\]]kun la rab tu mkhas/_/de lta'i rnal 'byor nyung yang lnga/_/mang bar gyur na rnal 'byor kyang /_/bskyed de de ltar rigs par spyad/_/lnga gnyis zung du gnas pa las/_/bskyed pa'i rim pa mthar phyin pas/_/nang gi mchod pa brtsam par bya/_/de nas

[\[33a.3\]]pha yin rtsa rnams ma/_/rlung ni las kyi sems dpa' yin/_/de la sogs pa'i man ngag rnams/_/slob dpon zhal las shes par bya/_/'khor lo gsum la'ang de bzhin no/_/tshogs zhes bya ba mang po yin/_/'khor lo zhes bya ba skor du btub/_/mchog ces bya ba lhan

[\[40a.1\]]de 'og 'od zer dkar po'i rgyun/_/bdud rtsi lta bus lus khyab nas/_/gsos nas mchog tu gyur par bsam/_/yang na brgya rtsa rtsa ba'i sngags/_/bzlas pas gong bzhin sdig pa sbyong /_/yi ge brgya pa'i dbang por bsgyur/_/brgya rtsa sngags 'bum bzlas pa

[\[40b.1\]{D2184}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_karma kra ma nA ma muk+ti kA ba li/_bod skad du/_las kyi rim pa mu tig phreng ba zhes bya ba/_'jam pa'i dbyangs dang rdo rje bsnams/_/spyan ras gzigs la phyag 'tshal lo/_/sku gsung thugs kyi mthu ldan pas/_/nyon mongs gdung bzhi byed pa/_/

[\[40b.3\]]gyis ni/_/sems can don grub glegs bam med/_/de ltar rtsod pa'i dus su ni/_/po ti dag la brten gyur pas/_/bla mas dgongs pa'i po ti la/_/dga' ba chen po bskyed par bya/_/de nas ma ga gang zag la/_/ston pa thugs rje che ldan pas/_/sdud pa rdo rje gsang bdag la/_/

[\[40b.5\]]mtshungs pa/_/shin tu drin che gus pas bstod/_/sems can mun khang 'khyams pa la/_/mar me bstan pas lam rnyed bzhin/_/'khor bar 'khyams pa'i sems can la/_/man ngag rin chen 'di bstan pas/_/phyag rgya mchog gi lam rnyed 'gyur/_/de bas shin tu drin che bas/_/
[\[40b.6\]]yul zhing sne phran bcas pa dang /_/rin chen la sogs nor rdzas dang /_/bu dang chung ma bran 'khor bcas/_/srog lus man chad phul gyur kyang /_/bla ma'i sku drin 'khor mi 'gyur/_/de bas 'bad pa thams cad kyis/_/bla ma mnyes par mi byed na/_/man ngag thob kyang ltung bar 'gyur/_/
[\[40b.7\]]gzhan yang rgyud ni sna tshogs las/_/bstan pa bsrung ba'i don slad du/_/mthu yi sbyor ba'i man ngag rnams/_/dgos pa bsdus te bstan par bya/_/de lta'i bla ma rin chen la/_/gong ma bzhin du shes par bya/_/man ngag bstan pa'i slob ma la/_/rnam pa bzhi ru shes byas la/_/phyi

[\[41a.3\]]par bya/_/de yi rnal 'byor mos pa ni/_/mas mtha' thun tshod chung ngu gcig_/nyin zhag 'das na nyams par 'gyur/_/dang por bskyed rim bsgom pa ni/_/rim gyis sam ni cig car du/_/bskyed pa brtan par gyur pa'i chad/_/thun tshod chen po brtan pa dang /_/kha dog spros par shes

[\[41b.1\]]nas/_/snang ba mched par gyur pas su/_/kun rdzob sgyu ma ji bzhin pa/_/thugs su chud pa'i stobs kyis ni/_/lhan cig dga' ba la zhugs pas/_/spros med 'od gsal de bzhin thob/_/de nas rim gyis mthar thugs/_/thob par de ni ma gyur kyang /_/tshe dbang bsgrub pas thob

[\[42a\]]
[\[42a.1\]]mang po la ni rgyu ru 'dod/_/srog dang dbang po che zhes pa/_/ming gi rnam grangs nyid du 'dod/_/de yang rlung dang rtsa dang ni/_/byang chub sems su byas pas na/_/tha dad nyid du 'dod pa'ang yod/_/shes pa bsdus dang ma bsdus pa/_/gnas skabs don gyis 'jug
[\[42a.2\]]pa yin/_/tshe bsgrub pa'i cho ga ni/_rang gi snying gar 'od kyi gzhal yas khang /_/de yi dkyil na a dkar gnyis/_/phra 'dus zla ba kha sbyor gyur/_/de nas hUM gnyis 'phro 'du las/_/rdo rjer gyur pas steng 'og mnan/_/tshe rnams 'phrog pa'i 'byung po de/_/drag po sbyor ba la sogs
[\[42a.3\]]kyis/_/sngags brjod phyag rgya bcas nas su/_/bcom zhing brlag nas med par byas/_/lha mo'i sprul pas tshe rnams dgug_/sngags brjod phyag rgyas bkug nas kyang /_/bsrung zhing ye shes che yang dbab/_/dbab pa'i phyag rgya bcing ba ni/_/rdo rje sor mo nang bsnol te/_/mthe
[\[42a.4\]]bong gnyis kyi nang du dpe ba/_/oM badzra A yu She hUM/_A be sha ya A A/_lus la mar rim bzhin du bstim/_khyad par snying gi dkyil du bstim/_/baM yig dmar po 'phros pa las/_/man ngag la sogs sbyor bas bcing /_/bsdu zhing gzung ba'i man ngag ni/_/shes rab la sogs
[\[42a.5\]]thabs kyis bstan/_/tshe yi yon tan la sogs ni/_/rgyud la sogs las shes par bya/_/tshe dang dum bu rnam smin gsum/_/de gsum thabs sogs mthun pa yang /_/gcig la gcig bstan mdung khyim 'dra/_/yi ge gsum gyi man ngag kyang /_/gnas gsum dag tu
[\[42a.6\]]bcing ba yin/_/sbyor ba la sogs bcing bar bya/_/de ni tshe sgrub man ngag go/_/byang sems blang ba'i man ngag kyang /_/de yang rnal 'byor spyod pa yi/_/mkhas pas 'chi rtags shes nas ni/_/rin chen 'bar ba'i snod nang du/_/blangs nas mtshal chen dang sbyar nas/_/sbyor
[\[42a.7\]]ba'i stobs kyi shangs su 'phang /_/rnam shes rlung la zhon pa de/_/dang po rten dang bral tsam na/_/sngags bzlas 'od zer stobs kyis su/_/snying ga nyid du bcing bar bya/_/de nas snga ma'i rten la gzhug_/sbyor ba la sogs gzhan yang myur bar bya/_/gzhan yang gsang ba spyod pa ni/_/
[\[42b\]]
[\[42b.1\]]mdzad pa'i dus ni rnam gsum ste/_/dang po bdud rtsi spyod pa la/_/mos pas 'jug dang dngos la 'jug_/mos pas 'jug pa gzhan dang mthun/_/dngos su 'jug pa'i thabs bstan pa/_/bdud rtsi rtsa ba lnga btsal la/_/rang gi lus las btsal bar bya/_/btsal nas bsgrub pa'i
[\[42b.2\]]ri lu de/_/tshad du phyin nas bza' bar bya/_/bza' ba dang po rim gyis bslab/_/zas dang rjes zin rting nyid la/_/zhag gsum na ni ci ran bza'/_/btung ba'ang de bzhin de rting la/_/zhag lnga na ni bza' bar bya/_/de nas zla phyed zla gcig go/_/de rnams par gyi 'tsho ba ni/_/
[\[42b.3\]]nang gi bdud rtsi slar bsdams la/_/bza' zhing btung ba nyid du bya/_/de rnams bag la zha nas ni/_/bar bar gong bzhin bza' bar bya/_/yang na rim bzhin de bzhin lnga ba/_/de nas nang gi rgyun bzlog gis/_/rim bzhin lus rnams gso bar bya/_/lus ni shin tu rgyas gyur na/_/
[\[42b.4\]]ting 'dzin bogs ni skye bar 'gyur/_/man ngag stobs kyis zhugs pa yis/_/mi rtog ye shes skye bar 'gyur/_/yang na bogs ni dbyung ba'i thabs/_/nang gi gso thabs spo ba dang /_/phyi yi gso thabs spo ba dang /_/lus la rdzas rnams byugs pa yis/_/ting 'dzin bogs
[\[42b.5\]]rnams skye bar 'gyur/_/thabs des skye bar ma gyur na/_/man ngag bsgom pas spo bar bya/_/des kyang skye bar ma gyur na/_/gnas la sogs pa spo bar bya/_/spos kyang skye bar ma gyur na/_/'byung po'i gnod pa yod pa yin/_/'byung po bsal ba'i thabs rnams bya/_/
[\[42b.6\]]'byung po bsal kyang ma byung na/_/sngon gyi bag chags mthug pas ni/_/de nyid sbyang ba'i cho ga bya/_/des kyang skye bar ma gyur na/_/tha mi dad pa'i 'du shes kyis/_/dkyil 'khor la sogs spos pa yis/_/ting nge 'dzin ni skye bar 'gyur/_/des kyang skye bar ma gyur na/_/slob
[\[42b.7\]]dpon man ngag nyams pa yin/_/slob dpon dam tshig nyams pas kyang /_/man ngag mthu ni chung bar byed/_/ye shes skye ba'i gnas rnams ni/_/slob dpon dam tshig nyams sogs la/_/dam tshig la sogs nongs pa dang /_/rang gi man ngag nyams pa dang /_/dam tshig nyams
[\[43a\]]
[\[43a.1\]]pa'i the tshom zos/_/lta spyod nyams su ma lon dang /_/dus dang rtags sogs ma shes dang /_/man ngag bsgom rim ma shes dang /_/sbyang ba la sogs ma shes dang /_/sems 'dzin phra mo yod srid kyang /_/ye shes skye bar mi 'gyur ro/_/de rnams skyon spangs
[\[43a.2\]]yon tan ldan/_/de ni ye shes ma skyes kyang /_/tshogs chen khyad par bsags nas su/_/skye ba phyi mar ye shes kyi/_/nges pa don yin thogs med do/_/mtshan nyid la sogs gzhan dag tu/_/snga ma las kyi 'phel shugs kyis/_/ma nges pa dag bstan pa de/_/sngags kyi
[\[43a.3\]]nus mthu khyad par gyis/_/las kyi 'phen pa bcom nas kyang /_/skye ba phyi mar nges pa'i don/_/phyi mar rkyen sogs thams cad kun/_/nges pa kho nar 'dzom par 'gyur/_/de ru rkyen rnams gzhan 'gyur na/_/dge bar bsngo ba legs 'gyur bar/_/ma 'tsham skye ba bdun la

[\[43a.5\]]'gor ba yin/_/de dag kun la rab 'bring gsum/_/ring dang myur dang shin tu myur/_/gsang sngags la la'i gzhung dang ni/_/slob dpon la la'i gzhung gis ni/_/bcud kyis len gyi man ngag gis/_/lus sems las su rung gyur nas/_/man ngag stobs kyis ye shes
[\[43a.6\]]skye/_/des ni phyag rgya'i dngos grub thob/_/phyag rgya mchog ni 'dod pa na/_/tshe la dbang sgyur bsgrubs nas ni/_/man ngag bsgoms pa'i stobs kyis ni/_/phyag rgya mchog ni thob par 'gyur/_/slob dpon la la'i gzhung gis ni/_/bskyed rim brtan par gyur pa dang /_/
[\[43a.7\]]bcud kyis len gyi man ngag bsgrub/_/des ni tshe la dbang sgyur 'grub/_/tshe dbang thob pa des kyang ni/_/phyag rgya phyag rgya mchog gnyis thob/_/bcud kyis len gyi man ngag kyang /_/mkha' 'gro'i rgyud du shes par gyis/_/phyag rgya mchog gi man ngag cung zhig tsam/_/rnyed par
[\[43b\]]
[\[43b.1\]]bya ba'i lus kyi phreng ba thabs kyi rim pa bkod pa'o/_/gzhan yang /_/bstan pa bsrung ba'i don slad du/_/las kyi phreng ba gzhan yang bstan/_/bdag nyid lhag pa'i lhar bskyed la/_/mdun du mgon po nag po ni/_/sku gsung thugs las byung ba yi/_/hUM de nyid las bskyed pa

[\[43b.3\]]bzlas pa'i man ngag ni/_/oM ma hA kA la ha na ha na badzre na swA hA/_bzlas pa yi ni man ngag kyang /_/rten dang brten pa'i gnas tshul des/_/gru gsum gzhal yas sgo gcig pa/_/de yi bdag po rigs dang bstun/_/'phro 'du bya ba'i tshul rnams kyang /_/'khor lo tsha tsha gdab
[\[43b.4\]]pa'i tshul/_/lce yang rigs dang bstun pa yin/_/ngag gi bzlas pa byed tshul yang /_/nyi ma shar dang ru chu brug_/de yi bzlas pa'i grangs rnams kyang /_/sum 'bum drug 'bum sa ya ru/_/bzlas pa byas pas mtshan ma rnyed/_/des su 'byung bar ma gyur na/_/sbyang ba byas te
[\[43b.5\]]bzla bar bya/_/sngags kyi nus pa che chung dang /_/mos pa yi ni khyad par dang /_/bag chags che chung khyad par gyis/_/rdo rje drag po'i rgyud rnams las/_/sngags kyi sbyor ba gzhan dag gis/_/bsnyen dang gsad pa'i las rnams bya/_/lha yi sbyor ba spo ba yang /_/de bzhin du

[\[44a.1\]]ban+d+ha/_ha na ha na/_da ha da ha/_pa tsa pa tsa/_di na mi ke na hUM hUM phaT/_hUM b+ha ga pA na/_oM bi laM ba hUM hUM phaT/_oM g+hu swA hA/_gsang ba'i sngags so/_/oM b+h+rUM/_mngon spyod kyi'o/_/oM dzr-IM swA hA/_dbye ba'o/_/oM khaM swA hA/_bskrad pa'o/_/oM hUM swA hA/_dgug pa'o/_/oM

[\[44a.7\]]'di ni bsam pa tsam gyis kyang /_/sangs rgyas nyid kyang nges par 'jig_/ma hA kA la'i rnal 'byor gyis/_/gdug pa khro bo'i sems kyis ni/_/de yi lte ba'i rtsa ba la/_/rnal 'byor can gyis lag pa gcad/_/ming gi yi ge dang po las/_/gsad bya mdun du bsam
[\[44b\]]
[\[44b.1\]]par bya/_/rnam shes de la bcug nas ni/_/kha sbyar nang nas gnas mthong nas/_/de phyung srog dang dbral mthong nas/_/ro ni dum bu stong du gtub/_/bza' 'am yang na gtor ma bya/_/de ma thag tu spyi gtsug bsam/_/khrag skyugs 'dar zhing mgo skyes kyang /_/kha ni thur

[\[46b.1\]]dang nyi shu rtsa gcig dang /_/zla ba dang gcig gi bar du bsgrub/_/de nas 'khor lo ldan pa'am/_/shugs dang ldan pa'i sbyor ba yis/_/shin tu myur bar 'phang bar bya/_/de nyid bskor ba'i tshul du'am/_/ri mo'i tshul du byas pa yis/_/ting 'dzin sbyor ba'ang de bzhin bsam/_/oM
[\[46b.2\]]shwA sa gA pa ye hUM che ge mo sha tU na mA ra ya hUM phaT/_yang na drag po'i 'brub khung du/_/tsher ma can gyi shid bkang ste/_/raM las drag po'i me dpung bsam/_/gro ga 'am ni shing shun la/_/bsgrub bya'i ming ni bris nas kyang /_/khri'am 'bum du bzlas nas ni/_/bsgrub bya bkug

[\[46b.4\]]las 'di brtsam par bya/_/dmar zhing chags pa'i rang bzhin can/_/khog pa'i rten ni btsal bar bya/_/'od ma'i gzhu ni lta bu yi/_/dkyil du de nyid bzhag nas kyang /_/dus la de ni bab pa yi/_/smin byed dang po rgyug pa dang /_/mdongs dang ldan pa'i mtshal chen gnyis/_/bsres

[\[50b.5\]]pa la/_/bshad tshul bzhi yis bum pa'i dbang /_/dngos su dga' ba'i don la yang /_/dga' bde bzhi yi don tshang bas/_/bum pa'i dbang bzhi de la sbyar/_/mgrin pa longs spyod 'khor lo la/_/rtsa rlung rten dang brten pa la/_/shes pa'i dbang ni tshul bzhin bshad/_/de ni mchog

[\[80b.2\]]dkyil 'khor bri ba'i las kyis zhes/_/zer zhing sa la thim par 'gyur/_/ro bsal nyes pa spangs pa ste/_/'thas par bcag cing rnam lnga dang /_/dbugs 'byung gis ni byung par bya/_/yang na me yi las kyis sbyang /_/stong pa'i sngags kyis byin brlabs te/_/rim pas
[\[80b.3\]]lha yi khang par bsam/_/me tog steng du rdo rje bzhag_/bla mas khrus byas rdo rje 'chang /_/bskyed pa'i yan lag kun rdzogs pas/_/shar bltas dkyil 'khor steng 'dug la/_/tshad med bzhi yis gzhan don bsgrub/_/rnam rgyal la sogs bskyed pa yi/_/slob ma gus pas
[\[80b.4\]]spos thogs la/_/mchod la tshig 'di brjod par bya/_/hUM byams pa chen po rdo rje 'dzin/_/zhe sdang dag pas me long ye shes gsal/_/gtum po gdug pa 'dul mdzad pa/_/rdo rje bsnams la phyag 'tshal lo/_/de bzhin gshegs pa kun zhi ba/_/de bzhin gshegs pa
[\[80b.5\]]ma lus gnas/_/chos kun bdag dang bral ba'i mchog_/dkyil 'khor dam pa bzhengs su gsol/_/de bzhin lho phyogs la sogs nas/_/hUM snying rje chen po rdo rje 'dzin/_/nga rgyal dag pa mnyam nyid ye shes mchog_/gtum po gdug pa 'dul mdzad pa/_/rdo rje
[\[80b.6\]]bsnams la phyag 'tshal lo/_/mtshan rnams yongs su rdzogs pa yi/_/mtshan min thams cad spangs pa ste/_/kun du bzang po sku yi mchog_/dkyil 'khor dam pa bzhengs su gsol/_/hUM dga' ba chen po rdo rje 'dzin/_/'dod chags dag pa so sor rtog_/gtum po
[\[80b.7\]]gdug pa kun 'dul ba/_/rdo rje bsnams la phyag 'tshal lo/_/zhi ba mchog gi chos chen po/_/ye shes spyod pa rnam spyod pa/_/kun du bzang po gsung gi mchog_/dkyil 'khor dam pa bzhengs su gsol/_/hUM btang snyoms chen po rdo rje 'dzin/_/gti mug rnam dag nan
[\[81a\]]
[\[81a.1\]]tan ye shes mchog_/gtum po gdug pa kun 'dul ba/_/rdo rje bsnams la phyag 'tshal lo/_/sems can kun gyi srog chen po/_/rang bzhin rnam dag dri ma med/_/kun du bzang po thugs kyi mchog_/dkyil 'khor dam pa bzhengs su gsol/_/
[\[81a.2\]]de nas rdo rje slob dpon gyis/_/khro zhing brjid pa'i skur byas te/_/rkang pa hUM las rdo rje bsam/_/mig gnyis nyi zla 'bar ba ste/_/rdo rje dril bu'i phyag rgya yis/_/'jigs spangs byang shar mtshams song la/_/rang gis bstod cing nga rgyal gyis/_/hUM dkyil 'khor sa gzhi la
[\[81a.3\]]gnas pa'i/_/lha tshogs bgegs tshogs kun nyon cig_/nga ni dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzin/_/nga yi bka' las ma 'da' bar/_/bgegs kyi tshogs rnams 'gro bar gyis/_/gal te khyed rnams mi 'gro na/_/ye shes rdo rje 'bar ba yis/_/mgo bo tshal pa brgyar
[\[81a.4\]]'gas shing /_/lus rnams stong du gyur nas ni/_/rnam par 'joms par gdon mi za/_/de bas khyed rnams gzhan du dengs/_oM badzra tsaN+Da ma hA ro Sha Na sarba big+h+nAn uts+tsha ta ya phaT/_ces pas bgegs rnams bskrad par bya/_/gar stabs kyis ni bskor ba dang /_dang por
[\[81a.5\]]phyin la 'di skad brjod/_/gang dag mi 'gro bgegs yod na/_/lus ngag yid kyi nus pa rnams/_/gzhom phyir khro bo'i phur bus gdab/_/kI la ya zhes btab nas kyang /_/A ko Ta yas brdung bar bya/_/me ri la sogs sngags kyis bsrung /_/gtso bo'i gdon ni gru bzhi ste/_/
[\[81a.6\]]'khor lo dri chus zlum por bya/_/kha dog mthun pa'i me tog dgram/_/sa yi cho ga rdzogs pa dang /_/lha ni lhag par gnas par bya/_/rang sar lha rnams rdzogs pa dang /_/mchod bstod me tog spos thogs la/_/hUM dus gsum bde gshegs thams cad kyi/_/thugs kyi sras
[\[81a.7\]]po rdo rje 'chang /_/dpa' bo rdo rje bde mas 'khyud/_/'khor gyi khro bo ma lus kun/_/kun nas bdag la dgongs nas kyang /_/khyed rnams la yang mchod pa dang /_/slob ma rnams la phan pa'i phyir/_/rdo rje can bdag che ge zhes/_/dkyil 'khor dam pa bzhengs su gsol/_/rjes su brtse
[\[81b\]]
[\[81b.1\]]bas nyer dgongs te/_/song ni dgyes pas byon par mdzod/_/gzhan yang gsang sngags lha rnams dang /_/'jig rten skyong ba ma lus dang /_/rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems bskyed rnams/_/sangs rgyas bstan pa'i chos skyong rnams/_/gang dag rdo rje'i spyan ldan pa/_/rdo
[\[81b.2\]]rje 'chang gi dkyil 'khor mchog_/deng bdag 'dri bar gyur pa la/_/bdag dang skal ldan slob ma rnams/_/byin gyis brlab phyir bsrung bar mdzod/_/bum pa lhag par gnas 'dod pas/_/rin chen 'byung khungs las byung ba/_/dri ma med cing lto ba che/_/mgrin phra mchu
[\[81b.3\]]'phyang dri zhim chus/_/dkar zhal byas nas mtshan ma dgod/_/rnam rgyal phyag mtshan rdzogs par bri/_/bskrad cing chu dang byang sems dang /_/byA g+h+ra sing ha dbyig pa dang /_/ut+pal gzhan gyis mi thub pa/_/ha sa de ba gser dngul dang /_/mu tig mu men bye ru gzhug_/nas
[\[81b.4\]]til gro sran mung+ga dang /_/ga pur dzA ti gur gum mchog_/tsan+dan gnyis dang a ga ru/_/mar dang bu ram sbrang rtsi dang /_/lan tshwa rnams kyis lto ba dgang /_/gos kyis mgrin pa bkab pa dang /_/tsu ta la sogs 'bras bu can/_/yang na me tog yod pas brgyan/_/me
[\[81b.5\]]tog ldan pa'i ra stegs sam/_/ku sha'i gdan la rang sar bzhugs/_/bum pa b+h+rUM las gzhal yas khang /_/chu skyes nyi zla'i gdan bcas pa/_/rnam rgyal lha rnams tshogs par bskyed/_/gzhan du sa bon gang yin pas/_/cho ga ma lus rdzogs par bskyed/_/hUM khro bo
[\[81b.6\]]gtum po gdug pa 'dul/_/rang bzhin ye shes lnga yi dngos/_/rnam dag dri med sku 'chang ba/_/'gro don mdzad la phyag 'tshal lo/_/bde gshegs sku la gnyis med 'khyud/_/stong pa nyid kyi bde ster ma/_/dmar ljang gri gug thod pa 'dzin/_/dpa' mo bde ma phyag
[\[81b.7\]]'tshal lo/_/sku gsung thugs dang phrin las kyi/_/gtso bo khro chen 'jigs pa che/_/gdug pa tshar gcod 'jigs pa'i sku/_/phyogs kyi khro bo phyag 'tshal lo/_/mar me bdug spos dri chab ma/_/zhal zas kyis ni tshim byed pa/_/mchod pa'i lha mo dgos 'dod 'byung /_/
[\[82a\]]
[\[82a.1\]]mtshams su bzhugs la phyag 'tshal lo/_/lcags kyu zhags pa lcags sgrog ma/_/dgyes pa'i dril bu sgrog mdzad ma/_/khro mo dbang phyug chen mo rnams/_/sgom bzhi la phyag 'tshal lo/_/bstod cing srad bu dang ldan pas/_/phrin las sbyar zhing bzlas
[\[82a.2\]]par bya/_/gtor mas mchod cing gsol ba btab/_/slob ma lhag par gnas pa yang /_/bsrung zhing mdzes pa'i me tog thogs/_/khrus byas gtsang ma'i gos ldan zhing /_/dga' ba'i sems kyis gsol ba gdab/_/dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa che/_/byang chub
[\[82a.3\]]chen po'i tshul bstan pa/_/mgon po chen po bdag 'tshal lo/_/dam tshig de nyid bdag la stsol/_/byang chub sems mchog bdag la stsol/_/sangs rgyas chos dang dge 'dun te/_/skyabs gsum dag kyang bdag la stsol/_/thar pa chen
[\[82a.4\]]po'i grong mchog tu/_/mgon po bdag ni gzhug par mdzod/_/lan gsum bar du gsol ba gdab/_/'od kyis phur byas sdig pa sbyang /_/rjes su gzung bas spro ba ni/_/bu tshur theg pa chen po yi/_/tshul chen snod ni khyod yin te/_/gsang sngags spyod tshul cho ga mchog/_

[\[82a.6\]]sems can la/_/snying rje chen po rab bskyed nas/_/bsgral zhing grol ba'i lam la bkod/_/bde bar dbugs ni dbyung bar gyis/_/slob ma'i tshogs kyis sdig bshags la/_/dge bsnyen la sogs rim pas sbyin/_/gang yin bslab pa bstan pa dang /_/slob ma lhar
[\[82a.7\]]byas yang na ni/_/gnas gsum lhar bcas rtags btab la/_/bla ma dkon mchog gsum po dang /_/bcom ldan phyag na rdo rje ni/_/'khor bcas ma lus thams cad kyang /_/bdag la dgongs nas gzigs su gsol/_/bdag gis thog ma med pa nas/_/sdig pa
[\[82b\]]
[\[82b.1\]]bgyis pa ma lus kun/_/bcom ldan phyag na rdo rje yi/_/spyan sngar da lta mthol zhing bshags/_/bla ma dkon mchog gsum po dang /_/sangs rgyas kun bdag rdo rje can/_/de rigs 'dzin pa'i rnal 'byor rnams/_/dge ba mdzad la rjes yi rang /_/bcom ldan
[\[82b.2\]]phyag na rdo rje ni/_/dus gsum bde gshegs thams cad kyi/_/gsang sngags bdag pos dbang bskur la/_/gsang sngags 'khor lo bskor bar bskul/_/mthu ldan skyon med khyed rnams la/_/skye rgas na 'chi mi mnga' yang /_/'gro ba'i don du sku sprul pa/_/
[\[82b.3\]]mthun 'jug mya ngan mi 'da' gsol/_/don dam rang bzhin mtshan ma med/_/mtshan mar mi rtog chos sku la/_/bde gshegs mtshan dpe'i skur snang ba/_/rdo rje can la skyabs su mchi/_/dus gsum mgon po thugs rje can/_/byams pa'i thugs las ma g.yos kyang /_/
[\[82b.4\]]dgongs pa'i dbang gis khro sprul la/_/gsang sngags lha tshogs kun skyabs mchi/_/de sgrub des mtshon gsung gi chos/_/nyi shu rtsa brgyad drag po'i tshogs/_/chos kyi rang bzhin dri ma med/_/chos kyi mchog la skyabs su mchi/_/sna tshogs skur sprul don mchog bsgrub/_/
[\[82b.5\]]rin chen skyabs mchog dge 'dun dang /_/'phags pa gos sngon byang chub sems/_/dge 'dun mchog la skyabs su mchi/_/bla ma dus gsum mgon po dang /_bcom ldan phyag na rdo rje ni/_/'khor dang bcas la lus 'bul bas/_/bzhes nas bdag la rjes brtse bas/_/
[\[82b.6\]]rjes su mthun pa'i dngos grub stsol/_/dang po byang chub sems bskyed nas/_/tshogs gnyis las byung dge ba rnams/_/'khor ba'i sems can ma lus don/_/byang chub chen por bsngo bar bya/_/byang chub tu yang sems bskyed la/_/sngags kyi dam tshig sbyin par bya/_/maN+Dal
[\[82b.7\]]sngon du 'gro ba yis/_/bla ma rdo rje slob dpon dang /_/bcom ldan rdo rje gtum po dang /_/dkon mchog gsum dang bstan dga' kun/_/bdag la dgongs nas gzigs su gsol/_/bdag ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di/_/dus 'di nyid nas bzung nas su/_/byang
[\[83a\]]
[\[83a.1\]]chub snying por mchis kyi bar/_/sems can kun gyi don gyi phyir/_/bla na med pa'i byang chub sems/_/dam pa bdag gis bskyed par bgyi/_/ji ltar dus gsum mgon po rnams/_/byang chub tu ni nges gnas pa/_/tshul khrims rnam gsum sdom pa
[\[83a.2\]]dang /_/dge ba'i chos ni sdud pa dang /_/sems can don byed tshul khrims rnams/_/so sor bdag gis gzung bar bya/_/bla na med pa'i dkon mchog gsum/_/sangs rgyas chos dang dge 'dun te/_/dam pa bdag gis bskyed par bgyi/_/'di ni sangs rgyas rigs
[\[83a.3\]]dag pa'i/_/dam tshig yin par rgyal bas bsgrags/_/rdo rje dril bu phyag rgya dang /_/skyon bral rdo rje chen po'i rigs/_/thugs rjes 'brel ba'i slob dpon ni/_/yang dag nyid du gzung bar bya/_/dri ma med pa'i dam tshig chos/_/rin chen rigs mchog chen po la/_/nyin re
[\[83a.4\]]bzhin du dus drug tu/_/sbyin pa rnam bzhi sbyin par bya/_/byang chub chen po las byung ba/_/pad+ma'i rigs mchog dag pa la/_/phyi nang gsang ba theg pa gsum/_/yang dag nyid du gzung bar bya/_/las kyi rigs kyi dam tshig ni/_/thun mong thun mong ma yin pa'i/_/sdom pa ma
[\[83a.5\]]lus thams cad kun/_/de bzhin nyid du so sor gzung /_/byang chub snying por mchis kyi bar/_/mchod pa'i las ni ci nus bgyi/_/ma bsgral ba ni bdag gis bsgral/_/ma grol ba ni bdag gis dgrol/_/dbugs ma phyin pa dbugs phyung bgyi/_/sems can dngos grub
[\[83a.6\]]che la dgod/_/dkyil 'khor me tog sngon por bcas/_/rdo rje 'chang la dbul bar bya/_/bdud rtsi rnam lnga gtor ma'i tshogs/_/rnam pa kun du bsten par bya/_/thabs kyis bsgral ba'i dam tshig ni/_/snying rje las byung bsgral bar bya/_/lan gsum bar du dam bcas pa/_/
[\[83a.7\]]rigs kyi lha las 'od 'phros pas/_/rang rang ye shes yig bzhis bstim/_/rdo rje khu tshur dri yi chus/_/mas rim bzhin du brtan par bya/_/de rjes mchod pa spro bar bya/_/a shwat+tha dang pa la sha_/u du m+WA ra la sogs pa'i/_/sor bcu gnyis sam yang na brgyad/_/rtse
[\[83b\]]
[\[83b.1\]]mo me tog mdzes pas brgyan/_/dkyil 'khor 'dab brgyad rnam lngas byug_/shar bltas dbus su sos bzung nas/_/pad+ma'i phyag rgyas dor byas te/_/khyod ni dkyil 'khor dam pa 'dir/_/zhugs pa'i dngos grub brtag pa'i phyir/_/rnam shes dag pa'i so shing 'di/_/sos
[\[83b.2\]]bzung nas ni dbus su dor/_/bdag dang bla ma steng bltas nas/_/mchog gi dngos grub dam pa yin/_/phyogs su phyin las so so ste/_/mtshams su 'jig rten dngos grub 'byung /_/thur bltas sa 'og grub pa yin/_/sa la ma lhung mkha' spyod do/_/bdud rtsi byin brlabs thod par
[\[83b.3\]]blugs/_/rdo rje 'di ni rdo rje'i chu/_/'thungs shig dam tshig byin gyis brlabs/_/gal te dam tshig 'das pa na/_/dmyal bar nges par sreg par byed/_/oM hrIHbi shud+d+ha d+harmA sarba bA paM ni sh+tsa/_sho ya bi kAlpAn a pa na ya hUM hUM/_lan gsum skyor chus ngag dag byas/_/lha dang rjes mthun
[\[83b.4\]]skud pa la/_/sngags btab g.yas dang phrin las g.yon/_/khro bo gtum po'i byin rlabs dang /_gsang sngags nus pa bla na med/_/skal ldan bar chad med par bsrung /_/su yang gnod pa ma byed cig_/ku sha gtsang ma byin brlabs te/_/bzhin bzangs tshur nyon dkyil
[\[83b.5\]]'khor du/_/'jug pa'i rtags rnams brtag pa'i phyir/_/ku sha'i rtswa 'di sngas dang stan/_/thub pas ting 'dzin grub ltar shog_/ma nor seng ge bzhin nyal nas/_/mtshan ma ji ltar byung ba ltar/_/bla ma'i mdun du brjod par bya/_/bzang na dngos grub spro ba bskyed/_/gal te ngan
[\[83b.6\]]na bskrad dang bsrung /_/me yi las kyis bzlog par bya/_/gzhan yang dge ba'i las kun shis/_/bla mas rdo rje can khyod la/_/nang par langs te dkyil 'khor pa/_/nam mkhar bteg la thig gad pa ste/_/bu mo gtsang zhing sdom ldan gyis/_/bkal ba ras bal las byung ba/_/
[\[83b.7\]]ye shes lnga ni gcig bsdus pa'am/_/yang na sku gsung thugs kyang rung /_/oM a n+yo n+ya a nu ga ta sarba d+harmA spa ra s+pha ra a nu ga ta sarba d+harmA t+yan+ta a nu pra biSh+Ti sarba d+harmAH/_zhes brjod pas ni bsgril par bya/_/pad+ma'i snod du bzhag nas kyang /_/mi 'chi lnga yis spangs byas la/_/blo ldan
[\[84a\]]
[\[84a.1\]]ye shes bstim byas la/_/nam mkhar ye shes dza dzas gdab/_/sgo yi bcu gnyis cha dang ldan/_/srid kyang khang pa nyis 'gyur la/_/tshangs pa'i las thig drang byas nas/_/oM badzra sa ma ya sU traM mA ti kra ma hUM/_/tshangs dang zur thig la sogs pa/_/
[\[84a.2\]]bstan bcos mthong zhing blo ldan des/_/cha ni gang yin rnam par dbye/_/gal te nyes pa'i 'bras bu ni/_/chad na bla ma'i srog g.yo zhing /_/dman lhag nad kyis btab par 'gyur/_/phyogs 'khrul slob ma rmongs par 'gyur/_/blo ldan nyes pa med par bya/_/gru bzhi sgo dang rta
[\[84a.3\]]babs bcas/_/dra ba dra ba phyed pas brgyan/_/nyi zla dril bu g.yer khas spras/_/pad+ma khyams dang rdo rje'i phreng /_/dur khrod me ri la sogs pa/_/rnam pa ma lus rdzogs par bya/_/rin chen rnam lnga 'bru phye dang /_/'byung khungs las byung rnam pa lnga/_/pad+mar so sor gzhag byas te/_
[\[84a.4\]]sngags kyis btab pa yig 'bru bsam/_/ye shes bstims la yig gsum gyis/_/byin gyis brlabs te mthing ga blangs/_/dbang ldan mtshams su drang bya ste/_/'di ni chos dbyings dag pa ste/_/sems can khams ni sgrol byed pa/_/dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa gnas/_/
[\[84a.5\]]de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gnas/_/de bzhin ljang gu drang byas la/_/'di ni so sor rtog pa dag_/dmar po mnyam nyid ye shes te/_/ser po bya ba grub pa la/_/dkar po me long ye shes dag_/me tog dor la mtshan ma brtag_/thams cad g.yas skor ma nor bar/_/sbom phra chad pa med par bri/_/nyes
[\[84a.6\]]pa 'byung ba'i rim pa ni/_/tshon mi mnyam zhing yo dang dma'/_/dngos grub nyams par 'gyur ba yin/_/yon pos rtsod la gdung bar 'gyur/_/sbom na nad 'byung gal te phra/_/nor nyams chad par gyur pas na/_/'chi 'gyur phyogs nyams phur bus 'debs/_/shar dkar
[\[84a.7\]]lho ser nub phyogs dmar/_/byang phyogs in+d+ra nI la'i mdog_/lte ba mthon mthing 'khyil par bya/_/mtshams sogs cho gas brtag pa dang /_/dur khrod rnams ni rim pas bri/_/rdo rje dkyil 'khor lhar bsgrub pa/_/yol bas bcad pa'i dkyil 'khor du/_/khrus byas
[\[84b\]]
[\[84b.1\]]dri yis lus byugs te/_/gos bzang gis brgyan lan gsum bskor/_/de nas rdo rje 'dzin pa yis/_/nga rgyal byas te hUM sgrogs pas/_/shar gyi sgo nas nang du zhugs/_/sgo bzhi yang ni dbye bar bya/_/oM badzra ud+g+ha Ta sa ma yA be sha ya hUM/_bum par rang gnas 'dug byas
[\[84b.2\]]te/_/mchod pa'i rdzas kyis legs brgyan nas/_/dkyil 'khor lha rnams rdzogs par bskyed/_/ye shes bstims la mchod par bya/_/bstod cing glu dang ldan pa yis/_/tshogs kyi 'khor los mchod par bya/_/de nas lhag pa'i lha yang bsdu/_/bzlas pa'i rim pa bzhin du brjod/_/
[\[84b.3\]]shar du zhi ba'i me las bya/_/de nas shar gyi dbang stegs la/_/slob ma'i cho ga ji lta bar/_/slob dpon dbang dang ldan par bya/_/me tog thogs la tshig 'di brjod/_/hUM thugs kyi sras po rdo rje 'dzin/_/gdug pa 'dul mdzad gtum po yis/_/slob ma smin par bya ba'i phyir/_/
[\[84b.4\]]bdag la dbang bskur sbyin par mdzod/_/de ltar rim pa rdzogs pa dang /_/de nas slob ma gzhug par bya/_/yol ba'i phyir gnas rim pa bzhin/_/khrus byas sngags 'dis dag par bsam/_/kA ya bAka tsit+ta sarba pA paM sho d+ha ni swA hA/_de nas lhar byas gnas gsum du/_oM badzra
[\[84b.5\]]ban+d+ha traT kA ya bAka tsit+ta/_zhes pas sdig pa dral byas la/_/rang rang yi ge bsam par bya/_/bgegs bskrad sdig pa gzhom pa dang /_/bla mas rang gi sa bon gyis/_/slob ma'i sdig pa sbyang bar bya/_/oM kA ya shud+d+ha sarba d+harmA kA ya shud+d+ho\u0f85haM/_oM bAka shud+d+ha sarba d+harmA
[\[84b.6\]]bAka shud+d+ho\u0f85haM/_oM tsit+ta shud+d+ha sarba d+harmA tsit+ta shud+d+ho\u0f85haM/_rnam dag lha yi ngo bor bya/_/gdong pa ras kyis bkab nas ni/_/bu khyod su yin ci la dga'/_/sangs rgyas kun gyi rang bzhin sku/_/slob dpon mgon la skyabs su mchi/_/gtso bo khro bor bcas pa yis/_/lha rnams
[\[84b.7\]]kun la phyag 'tshal lo/_/bdag ni skal bzangs rigs yin te/_/rdo rje 'dzin pa khyod la dga'/_/phrin las ma lus khyod la rdzogs/_/thar pa chen po'i grong khyer du/_/mgon pos bdag ni gzhug par mdzod/_/slob mas yon phul sngags 'di brjod/_/oM A khaM bI ra
[\[85a\]]
[\[85a.1\]]hUM/_rang rang gnas su bzhag nas kyang /_/bgegs kyi bar chad bsal bar bya/_/dkyil 'khor la ni bskor byas te/_/shar gyi phyogs nas sgo phye la/_/lha dang sangs rgyas rnams bskul te/_/sku gsung thugs kyi byin rlabs kyis/_/bdud bzhi rnam par
[\[85a.2\]]dag bcom nas/_/sngags 'dis phyag gsum brkyang la bya/_/oM na ma ste hUM/_oM na ma mi hUM/_na mo na ma hUM swA hA/_de nas thal sbyar shar phyogs nas oM trai lokya bi dza ya/_bU dzo pas+thA nA ya/_At+ma nAM ni R+YA ta yA mi/_sarba ta thA ga ta a k+Sho b+h+ya/_/a b+hi Shany+tsi a d+hi tiSh+Tha swa maM/_mi
[\[85a.3\]]bskyod brgya byin steng du gsal/_/oM ma hA kA la pU dzo pas+thA nA ya/_/At+ma nAM niR+YA ta yA mi/_sarba ta thA ga ta rat+na saM b+ha ba/_a b+hi Shany+tsi a d+hi tiSh+Tha swa maM/_lho yi phyogs nas phyag byas te/_/dpral bar sku ni khyab 'jug mnan/_/nub nas gsung gi dbang phyug gzhom/_/oM a mr-i ta kuN+Da
[\[85a.4\]]li/_pU dzo pas+thA nA ya/_At+ma nAM niR+YA ta yA mi/_sarba ta thA ge ta pad+ma d+ha ri/_a b+hi Shany+tsi a d+hi tiSh+Tha swa maM/_oM AR+ya dzaM b+ha la pU dzo pas+thA nA ya/_At+ma nAM ni R+YA ta yA mi/_sarba ta thA ga ta a mo g+ha sid+hi/_a b+hi Shany+tsi a d+hi tiSh+Tha swa maM/_nub byang rim pas phyag bya'o/_/las kyi bum pas khrus
[\[85a.5\]]byas te/_/sdom pa ma lus pa yang sbyin/_/byin gyis brlab phyir ye shes kyang /_/bla ma la ni gsol ba gdab/_/de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis/_/bdag la byin gyis brlab mdzod la/_/rdo rje sems dpa' bla na med/_/bdag la da lta bskyed du gsol/_/sdig bral spos kyis
[\[85a.6\]]bdug byas nas/_/'gying bcas rdo rje dril 'dzin pas/_/sangs rgyas ma lus lhag pa'i lhar/_/bsdus la gnyis med bde ba che/_/zag med bde bas yan lag khyab/_/hUM 'di ni rdo rje'i dam tshig ste/_/rdo rje gtum po sems dpa' che/_/ye shes rdo rje bla med 'di/_/da lta nyid du
[\[85a.7\]]'bab par shog_/oM badzra tsaN+Da ma hA ro Sha Na/_A be+e sha ya s+t+waM b+hA ya/_rA rA rA rA/_tsa lA ya/_a hUM ma hA dz+heM badzra tsaN+Da A be sha ya/_a a a a a/_zhes bzlas gang la babs gyur kyang /_oM badzra tsaN+Da ma hA ro Sha Na/_a d+hiSh+Thi te sa ma ya/_sngags kyis brtan byas lce la a/_/dge
[\[85b\]]
[\[85b.1\]]mi dge yi lung bstan bya/_/me tog rdo rje dang bcas pa/_/spyi bor bzhag la 'di skad brjod/_/hUM rdo rje gtum po deng khyod kyi/_/snying la yang dag zhugs pa ni/_/gal te tshul 'di gzhan smras na/_/de ma thag tu dral te gshegs/_/bdud rtsi lngas bkang ka pA lar/_/
[\[85b.2\]]sngags btab rdo rje dang bcas sbyin/_/hUM 'di ni khyod kyi rdo rje'i chu/_/dam tshig nyams na sreg par byad/_/dam tshig bsrungs na dngos grub rnams/_/rdo rje bdud rtsi'i chu 'dis 'grub/_/oM AHhUM badzrod ka Tha hUM/_/shar du 'dug la 'di skad brjod/_/de nas
[\[85b.3\]]brtsams te khyed rnams kyi/_/rdo rje gtum po nga yin gyi/_/khyed kyis nga la brnyas pa na/_/mi bde ma spangs dus byas nas/_/dmyal bar ltung bar gyur ta re/_/phyogs bzhi nas ni dngos grub brtag_/mdzes pa'i me tog lha la dor/_/gsang ba bla med me tog 'di/_/pho brang
[\[85b.4\]]dkyil 'khor lha mchog la/_/las dang rjes mthun brtse ba yis/_/rigs dang mthun par 'bab par shog_/pra tIts+tsha ho badzra/_lha yi stod dang rked pa dang /_/smad dang nye ring gtso 'khor gyi/_/bye brag dngos grub rtags yin no/_/de nas bla mas me tog blangs/_/slob ma'i mgor
[\[85b.5\]]bcings sngags 'di brjod/_/oM d+harma kuN+Da a b+hi Shiny+tsa/_lha bstim rigs kyi ming yang gzung /_/sngon gyi mig mkhan rgyal po yis/_/ma rig ling tog bsal ba ltar/_/de bzhin khyod kyi mig dbye ste/_/ye shes mig gis mthong bar shog_/badzra tsak+Shu pa tra laM hri/_/gdong
[\[85b.6\]]g.yogs bshus la 'di skad brjod/_/dkyil 'khor bzang po 'di la ltos/_/mthong na dad pa rab tu skye/_/khyod ni sangs rgyas rigs su gyur/_/sngags dang phyag rgyas byin brlabs te/_/dngos grub ma lus snod du 'gyur/_/rigs kyi rnam par dag pa bstan/_/de nas slob ma dad ldan

[\[86a\]]
[\[86a.1\]]sems can kun gyi don gyi phyir/_/bdag ni slob dpon mchog bgyid do/_/lan gsum brjod nas shar phyogs su/_/pad+ma 'dab brgyad khri la 'dug_/rnam rgyal bum pa la sogs pas/_/chu rnams thod pa'am bum par bsdus/_/rdo rje'i glu dang dril bur ldan/_/
[\[86a.2\]]rigs lnga rig pa'i lha mor ldan/_/bag chags ma lus dag byas te/_/sku gsum dam tshig las byung ba'i/_/ye shes bdud rtsi dri ma med/_/lha yi bdud rtsi rnam dag 'dis/_/mi bskyod rdo rje'i dbang bskur ro/_/oM A daR+sha dz+nyA na a b+hi Shiny+tsa hUM/_chu yi dbang bskur dam pa
[\[86a.3\]]'dis/_/sgrib pa rnam pa gsum bral nas/_/mi bskyod rnam dag ye shes 'thob/_/mi bskyod rdo rje dngos grub shog_/lugs ma'am thang ga 'bur bris pa'i/_/gser sogs dbu rgyan rin 'byung bsam/_/dbu rgyan rin chen dam pa 'dis/_/sems can tshim par byed pa'i mchog_/_
[\[86a.4\]]yid bzhin bsam pa 'grub byed pa/_/rdzogs sangs rgyas su dbang bskur ro/_/oM badzra sa man+tA dz+nyA na hUM tiSh+Tha a b+hi Shiny+tsa hUM/_dbu rgyan dbang bskur dam pa 'dis/_/rigs lnga'i sangs rgyas bde bar gshegs/_/bdag gi mgo la brgyan gyur te/_/rin chen 'byung ldan dngos grub
[\[86a.5\]]shog_/rin chen la sogs rdo rje la/_/snang ba mtha' yas bcug byas la/_/lag tu gtang la tshig 'di brjod/_/sangs rgyas kun gyi rdo rje'i dbang /_/mi phyed rnam dag 'od gsal stong /_/dam chos 'byung ba'i sgor gyur pa/_/rdo rje chos kyi dbang bskur ro/_/oM badzra pra ti be sha ya
[\[86a.6\]]dz+nyA na a b+hi Shiny+tsa hUM/_rdo rje'i dbang bskur dam pa 'dis/_/rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin/_/bdag gi rgyud la skyes gyur te/_/snang ba mtha' yas dngos grub shog_/dril bur don yod grub pa bcug_/lag pa g.yon gtad tshig 'di brjod/_/thabs dang shes rab ldan pa yis/_/
[\[86a.7\]]'gro don mnyam pa med byed pa/_/'dod pa'i phrin las rdzogs byed cing /_/dril bu las kyi dbang bskur ro/_/oM a d+hiSh+Tha na a nuSh+ThA na sid+d+hi dz+nyA na a b+hi Shiny+tsa hUM/_dril bu'i dbang bskur dam pa 'dis/_/dus gsum bde gshegs thams cad kyi/_/gsung gi dngos grub
[\[86b\]]
[\[86b.1\]]bdag gyur te/_/don yod grub pa'i dngos grub shog_/rnam snang bskyed la mtshog ma'i steng /_/'khor lo thogs pa'i ming sgrogs te/_/rdo rje ming gi dbang bskur bas/_/byang chub thob pa'i bar du ni/_/cis kyang gzhom par mi nus pas/_/rdo rje'i ming du rab tu grags/_/
[\[86b.2\]]oM pra ti shod+ha d+harma d+hA tu dz+nyA na nA ma a b+hi Shiny+tsA mi hUM/_ming gi dbang bskur dam pa 'dis/_/stong gsum bye ba phrag brgya ru/_/sprul pas 'gro rnams chos ston cing /_/rnam par snang mdzad dngos grub shog_/rigs lnga yum gyis ma rig lnga/_/rnam dag ye shes lnga sbyor bas/_/
[\[86b.3\]]rig pa'i dbang du rgyud pas bstan/_/shar du seng ge'i khri la 'dug_/steng du gdugs dkar phub nas kyang /_/phyir mi ldog pa'i dbang bskur te/_/slob dpon rang bzhin 'od dpag mchog_/skal ba chen po bdag la gsol/_/bde gshegs rnams kyi dbang bskur ni/_/
[\[86b.4\]]sangs rgyas byang chub rab bsgrub pa/_/de ni sangs rgyas dpag med do/_/brtul zhugs bla na med pa de/_/ji ltar 'dul bzhin bdag la gsol/_/de nas rnam rgyal bum pa blangs/_/steng 'og bzhag la tshig 'dis sbyin/_/dbang bskur rdo rje chen po ni/_/khams gsum

[\[87a\]]
[\[87a.1\]]byin la/_/'di de sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/_/rdo rje sems dpa'i phyag na bsnams/_/khyod kyis kyang ni rtag tu bcang /_/phyag na rdo rje'i brtul zhugs brtan/_/oM sarba ta thA ga ta sa ma ya tiSh+Tha e Sha s+t+waM d+ha ra ya mi hi hi hUM/_de nas dril bu sbyin byas te/_/'di ni

[\[87b\]]
[\[87b.1\]]gyis/_/de bzhin rigs kyis gang 'dul ba/_/khyod kyi phrin las mchog yin no/_/de nas slar yang rdo rje 'dzin/_/gsal bar byas te tshig 'di brjod/_/deng nas bzung nas rigs kyi bus/_/zhi rgyas nga dang gsad pa dang /_/dgug dang bcing dang bsreg pa dang /_/

[\[87b.3\]]dbyung rnams kyang sbyin/_/khyad par bkra shis dbang rnams kyang /_/rim pa bzhin du rdzogs par bya/_/gal te gsang ba'i dbang bskur ba/_/bzhin bzangs mig yangs lang tshor ldan/_/lus la dri yis byugs byas te/_/rtse dang dgod pas g.yo byas la/_/thabs dang
[\[87b.4\]]shes rab gnyis phab ste/_/nor bu byang chub sems ltung bas/_/bde gshegs khu ba mtheb srin gyis/_/drir bcas slob ma'i kha ru dbab/_/a ho su khas de btung ngo /_/rdo rje ro yis nyon mongs 'joms/_/mtshan ldan bde ba bskyed pa de/_/yol bas bar bcad
[\[87b.5\]]snyoms 'jug brtsam/_/bsrub dang srubs pa'i sbyor ba yis/_/sgra yi rgyun med longs spyod kyi/_/rlabs kyi rgyun ni chad pa las/_/lhan cig skyes pa ye shes kyang /_/rgyun gyi rnal 'byor dran par bya/_/skad cig de dang ma bral na/_/mi rtog ye shes skye bar 'gyur/_/de nyid brjod
[\[87b.6\]]du med pa la/_/brjod med tshig gi dbang du bshad/_/gal te de la mi rtog pas/_/bzhi pa dbang du rgyud du bstan/_/dkyil 'khor rnam lnga'i dbang bskur nas/_/tshogs dang mchod pa rgya chen bya/_/slob ma dad ldan mchog des kyang /_/rta dang glang po ma he dang /_/bu dang chung
[\[87b.7\]]ma srog dang dbyig_/ci yod phyag byas ma zhen pas/_/bla ma mnyes phyir dbul bar bya/_/bla mas slob ma dam pa'i mgor/_/bkra shis brjod cing gdugs phub pas/_/slob ma mchod pa rdzas thogs nas/_/drin len dkyil 'khor lan gsum bskor/_/smon lam

[\[88a.1\]]gdab cing dge ba bsngo/_/tho rangs tshon bsdus bum par blugs/_/chu'am ri'am nags phug sba/_/dri bzangs kyis ni thig phyis la/_/sa der zhi ba'i me las bya/_/yang na phongs pa tshim pa dang /_/tsai te'i las la brtson par bya/_/ji ltar rgyud las
[\[88a.2\]]gsal gyur cing /_/bla ma'i man ngag thob gyur kyang /_/cung zad spros phyir bdag nyid spro bar byas/_/'on kyang nyes tshogs ci mchis bshags par bya/_/bzang po mdor bsdus cho ga mchog_/gzhan phyir bkod pa'i dge ba yis/_/rigs drug gtum po'i lam zhugs nas/_/

[\[88a.5\]]gnas shing /_/thabs dang shes rab zung 'brel pa'i/_/mgon po sgrib pa kun spangs yon tan ma lus kun gyi bdag po de/_/shes rab thabs kyis mya ngan mtha' spangs nas/_/snying rje chen pos sems can mun 'thibs pa/_/mun ma mthong sgom rtsa ba nyon mongs zhi mdzad pa/_/

[\[88a.7\]]dang ldan/_/shAkya'i rigs kyi man ngag don ldan rgyas par bstan pa las/_/shes rab dmigs ma phyed pas bshad zin bstan pa dag_/de dag sman 'gyur 'dir ni gsal bar byas/_/des ni nyi zla dag dang mthun pa'i dam chos 'di/_/thugs rje nye bar bsngos pa yis/_/

[\[88b.1\]]snying rje ldan pa'i sems kyis su/_/rtsa rgyud man ngag bshad par bya/_/rtsa rgyud rang bzhin don rnams la/_/sde tshan lnga lnga nyi shu lnga/_/ya sha mtha' bcas rtsa ba ldan/_/thabs dang shes rab yi ge gnyis ldan gsum du 'dus/_/brjod bya rtogs byed tshig gi don/_/rtsa ba bshad dang

[\[88b.3\]]gyi don/_/thob byed rgyu 'bras gnyis kyi lam/_/dngos byed 'bras bu'i lam yin te/_/rgyu ni tshig de dran sogs pa'i/_/phyir zhing dro ba'i rang bzhin te/_/nyon mongs ma tshig zhi rtse mo'o/_/phyir mi ldog dang 'jig rten mthar stobs lnga/_/dbang po lnga yi rang bzhin no/_/byang chub yan
[\[88b.4\]]lag bdun po ni/_/mthong lam skad cig bcu drug go/_/sa dang bsgom lam mthar phyin 'bras bu'o/_/dngos byed lam ni 'bras bu sngags/_/byen gyis brlabs pas sngags mthu yon tan no/_/lam ma bgrod pas 'bras bu med/_/dper na gru gzings bskyod pa yis/_/rin
[\[88b.5\]]chen mchog ni thob par 'gyur/_/brjod bya ston pa'i tshig gis kyang /_/'bras bu bden pa myur du 'byin/_/des na sngags ni gsang sngags lam/_/lam ma bgrod par gsal byed 'gyur/_/des na brjod bya'i khyad kyi nus pa yin no/_/'di skad la sogs pa bshad pa mdzes par
[\[88b.6\]]bya ba'i phyir/_rgyud 'di par brjod bya dang /_dgos pa dang /_'brel pa dang /_mchog gi dgos pa bstan par bya ste/_brjod bya dngos po med pa'i tshig ni bstan kyang rtogs pa sngon du gtong ba rnams 'jug par mi 'gyur te/_dung la dkar po spyi ni 'jug gi bye brag la 'khrul
[\[88b.7\]]pa bzhin no/_/des na skyon yod pa'i phyir chos kyi rjes su 'brang ba rnams mi 'jug go/_/des na byis pa dang smyon pa dang mchog yin zhing gzhan la sogs pa ni dgos pa med snyam pa'am/_'di nyid kyi ma yin snyam pas mi 'jug ste/_tshig dang don thams cad kyi 'brel pa dang /_
[\[89a\]]
[\[89a.1\]]brjod bya dang /_dgos pa dang /_dgos pa'i yang dgos pa rnams gtan la phab pa sngon du byas nas mchod pas na/'di nyid 'brel pa la sogs pa yang brjod par bya'o/_/de bzhin du 'brel pa dang brjod pa bshad par cis te mi bya/_smyon pa'i tshig bzhin
[\[89a.2\]]du mi 'brel pa'am/_mo gsham la sogs pa la don med par 'dod pa'i zhen pas tshig chad par 'gyur bas ma ning gi gzugs la zhen pa'i 'dod pa rnams ci nas kyang tshig chad par 'gyur zhes brtags nas 'jug par mi 'gyur ba nyid do/_/de bas na 'jug pa'i yan
[\[89a.3\]]lag gi gtso bo yin pa'i phyir te/_thog ma nyid du dgos pa brjod par bya'o/_/de gang las shes par bya ba'i phyir/_dgos pa dang 'brel pa brjod par bya ba yang bstan to/_/de nas dgos pa'i dgos pa la sogs pa bstan to/_/brjod bya ji lta bu snyam pa la/_'di ltar lam
[\[89a.4\]]dang 'bras bu brjod bya'i 'bras bur rtog ces bya'o/_/brjod bya ni gnyis su med pa'i ye shes so/_/de yang sgras drangs nas blo la dngos su snang bas dngos kyi brjod bya zhes pa nas snang ba zhen pa'i brjod byas/_sgra drangs pa'i tshig gi /don 'dis brjod bya rtogs pas brjod bya
[\[89a.5\]]mtshon par byed pa'i tshig la yang brjod bya 'di'i don zhes 'brel par bya ste/_'di ltar lam la brten pas 'bras bu thob ste/_de ni de dang 'gal ba'i chos spong bar 'gyur ro/_/gal te de ltar yin du zad mod/_de nyid bstan pa ci phyir snyam nas des na 'dir sgra'i tshogs la ma brten par
[\[89a.6\]]nam yang rtogs pa mi 'byung ngo /_/ci'i phyir gal te byung na ni thams cad gzhung gi tshogs la sogs pa la mi ltos par 'gyur na ni don med do/_/gal te yod na thams cad skye ba'am/_rkyen med pa rtogs pa thar par gyur pa las/_rgyu med 'bras bu skye bar rigs pa med do/_/
[\[89a.7\]]nam mkha'i me tog bzhin no/_/des na rgyu la rang bzhin du bye brag gyur pa med pa las 'byung bar 'gyur ro/_/phyi ma ltar na yang 'ba' zhig pa rnams la ni 'ba' zhig rang las gzhan nus pa'i phyir mi 'byung ngo /_/'bras bu yan lag rgyu la ma tshang bar byung na ni/_dus thams
[\[89b\]]
[\[89b.1\]]cad du 'bras bu 'byung ste/_de ni med pa'i phyir ro/_/de bas na gzhung gi tshogs med na brjod bya'i rtogs pa mi 'byung ngo /_/de bzhin du gzhung thabs yin pa dang gzhung yang brjod bya'i don rtogs pa thabs las 'byung ba'i 'brel pa'o/_/de bas na gzhung gi tshogs
[\[89b.2\]]'di brjod bya shugs kyis rtogs bya yin la/_dgos pa ni thabs las 'byung ba yin la/_nyid kyis 'brel te de dag rang nyid kyis 'brel pa'o/_/de'i phyir gzhung bstan pas blang dor ni dgos pa yin no/_/des cir 'gyur zhe na/_rang gi don phun sum tshogs par 'gyur te/_
[\[89b.3\]]lam gyi rim pas tshogs lam dang drod la sogs par 'byung ngo /_/tshu rol gyi ye shes dang mthong sgom la sogs pas 'brel zhes te de ni mthar phyin pa yang bzung ste/_rigs kyi bu rnams dgos pa'o/_/de ni me dang du ba bzhin du de dang de las 'byung ba'i 'brel pa ste/_/thabs dang
[\[89b.4\]]thabs las 'byung ba'i tshul gyis 'brel pa'o/_/des na nyon mongs pa dang shes bya rtsa nas byang ba ni rang don no/_/'brel pa la yang de nyid do/_/sa bon dang bcas pa ston pa ni rang don phun sum tshogs pa'o/_/des na dgos pa'i dgos pa yang /_/gzhan la brten gzhan mu
[\[89b.5\]]stegs dang /_/nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas dang /_byang chub sems dpa' dang /_phyag rgya chen pos gzhan mthar phyin pa la sogs pa ni/_dgos pa'i dgos pa'o/_/des na chos kyi rjes su 'brang ba rnams la ni/_rgyud 'di brjod bya'i 'brel pa dang /_dgos pa'i dgos
[\[89b.6\]]pa bstan to/_/de nas brjod bya dang 'brel pa dang /_dgos pa dang 'bras bu dgos pa'i dgos pa la sogs pa bzhi nges par bstan to/_/gang zag dad pa'i rjes su 'brang ba rnams ni/_srid pa'i mtsho nges par bzung nas/_sangs rgyas kyi bka' nges par 'jug pa'i phyir
[\[89b.7\]]bstan mi dgos so/_/de ltar brjod bya dang dgos pa brjod nas/_yan lag bstan pa ni gzhung don to/_/de la 'di skad bdag gis thos pa zhes pa la sogs pa smos te/_sbud pa po'i tshig tu smos te/_'di skad smras pa thos zhes sbyar ro/_/'di'i tshe 'dis thos/_gzhan
[\[90a\]]
[\[90a.1\]]gyi tshe gzhan gyis thos par bstan to/_/thos pa ni bdag kho nas thos te/_gzhan dang 'brel pa med de/_de ni gzhan thos pa'o/_/'di ni ri rab rtse rtsa rgyud nyi khri sum stong kha nas thos pa'o/_/des ni thos par dka' ba dang /_thos pa mang ba la sogs pa yang
[\[90a.2\]]yongs su bzung ngo /_/gzhan ni bA rA Na sIr bden pa bzhi la sogs pa ste/_gzhan nye ba 'khor dang /_shA ri'i bu la sogs pa'i gtso 'khor tha dad pa'i phyir ro/_/'di skad bdag gis thos ni rgyal ba mar me mdzad dang /_shAkya thub pa dang /_gtso bo rdo rje 'chang dang /_rnam
[\[90a.3\]]rgyal la sogs pas las thos pa ste sngon dang da lta la sogs pa dang /_bar du yang thos pa ste/_gtso bo dang 'khor tha mi dad par bstan to/_/tha mi dad na rang gi tshig dang 'gal lo/_/gcig pa yin pa'i phyir snyam pa la/_gcig kyang mi sto ste/_kun rdzob tu snang ba thams cad kyang
[\[90a.4\]]'khrul pa mi bden pa sgyu ma yin pas don ni stong pa nyid kho na'o zhes rgyud las gsungs pa yin no/_/tha dad kyang mi 'gal te bde bar gshegs pa la skyon gnyis med de/_thams cad zhi ba mya ngan las 'das pa khams dang skye mched bral bas dus thams cad bdag dang bdag gis
[\[90a.5\]]stong pa nyid du med/_zla ba dang chu bzhin no/_/de bas khams gsum rnam par rgyal ba ni/_phyag na rdo rje nyid dang rang bzhin gcig pas/_byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gdul bya ni/_snang bas snang zhes bstan te me long rkyen gyis gzugs rang las gnyis su snang ba'o/_/de
[\[90a.6\]]bzhin du sems bskyed pa'i smon lam dang snying rje chen pos sems can gzhug pa'i ched du ston pa dang /_'khor dang ldan pa dang lam dang dri za'i gzugs dang /_phung po dang skye mched bcu gnyis dang /_khams dang rnam par byang pa'i 'bras bu dang /_nyon mongs pa dang /_mang
[\[90a.7\]]du bstan pa rnams ni/_sems can gzhug pa'i ched yin pas thos zhes bya/_gzhan nas theg pa bstan pa sems can gzhug pa'i ched du lags/_theg pa med cing 'bras bu med/_/ces gsungs so/_/des na phyag na rdo rje la khams gsum rnam par rgyal bas thos pa ste/_
[\[90b\]]
[\[90b.1\]]gtso 'khor tha mi dad par bstan to/_/gcig pa'i phyir thos pa dang 'gal snyam pa la/_mi 'gal te/_bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'chang phyag na rdo rjer snang la/_de yang khams gsum rnam par rgyal ba ru snang ngo //_/'o na de dngos su snang ngam mi snang ba yin/_sprul pa yin nam ma
[\[90b.2\]]sprul pa yin/_snang zhing sprul pa yin na sangs rgyas ma yin te/_dngos po tha dad du snang zhing shes pa gnyis dang ldan pa'i phyir ro/_/bcom ldan 'das ni log pa'i shes pa dang ste/_sa la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' dang khyad med do/_/de'i phyir de ni sangs rgyas su blta
[\[90b.3\]]bar mi bya'o/_/sprul pa ma yin na snang bar mi rigs so/_/ci'i phyir/_rgyu med 'bras bu snang ba'i phyir/_/ri bong rwa sogs snang bar rigs/_/zhes bya'o/_/bden te log pa'i shes pa dang ldan na de gnyis 'byung gi/_de med pa'i phyir de mi 'byung ngo /_/dngos su sprul yang mi sto
[\[90b.4\]]'dul ba'i dus la bab pa'i phyir/_de'i rang bzhin der snang ba'o/_/ma sprul yang rang nyid de'i tshe des 'dul la rnam par rgyal bar snang ba'o/_/de nas bka' la bar med pa'i phyir rang gis thos pa dang yang sdud pa pos thos zhes bya'o/_/'dir sems can gdul byas ma
[\[90b.5\]]rtogs par ston pa dang sdud pa po tha dad du bya ba med do/_/smon lam dang thugs rje dpag tu med pa'i 'gro don 'byung ba'i phyir thos zhes sbyar ro/_/des na skyon de gnyis mi 'byung ste/_de ni skyon thams cad dang bral ba'i phyir ro/_/dus kyang de ste bde'i tshe thos/_gzhan gyi tshe
[\[90b.6\]]gzhan thos pa ste dus kyang de'i tshe zhes bstan to/_/'di skad bdag gis thos pa ni e waM mA ya zhes 'byung bas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis 'byung ba lnga rigs dang ye shes lnga dang sgra dang skye mched dang /_khams bco brgyad dang /_g.yo ba dang /_mi g.yo ba dang /_rtsa
[\[90b.7\]]lnga dang dbang dang dga' ba la sogs pa la shes par bya'o/_/de dag bstan pa'i yan lag ni/_/phyi nang mthar thug rnam pa gsum/_/ci bzhin min dang ji bzhin sgra/_/dgongs pas bshad dang dgongs pa min/_/drang ba'i don dang nges pa'i don/_/phyi ni mi bzad dbyings
[\[91a\]]
[\[91a.1\]]dang sbyar/_/nang ni rtsa rlung byang chub sems/_/rtsa lnga gtum mo'i man ngag go/_/mthar thug mthong lam ye shes te/_/dpe ye shes gnyis med phyag rgya chen po'i lam bcu gnyis ni dngos po bral ba des na bral ba'i shes pa'o/_/gzhan yang phung po lnga
[\[91a.2\]]dang /_tshogs drug dang /_skye mched bcu gnyis dang /_khams dang /_bag chags rnams so/_/de ni/_brda min skye bo thal ba'i tshig_/dgos pa ma yin zhes su bya/_/shu kra su tra ma nu ha ra dang /_/tan+t+ra yan+t+ra man+t+ra'o/_/byang sems kyis sems can phal pa rnams
[\[91a.3\]]thugs rje zag bcas thams cad skyob pa'o/_/sngags dang shes pa ma lus yongs su 'dzin rgyud ni/_/'khor ba brgyud de chos nyid byang chub sems/_/'di yang gnas pa ma lus stong pas 'dzin par byed/_/lung las 'di lta ste/_ji lta ji ltar 'dul 'gyur bas/_/sems
[\[91a.4\]]can ma lus gsad par bya/_/ma byin len dang brdzun smra dang /_/de lta de ltar sems can don/_/'dod chags la sogs spang bas spyad/_/sems can kun la phan don du/_/sangs rgyas bstan pa rgyu yi phyir/_/sems can thams cad bsad na yang /_/de la sdig pas mi
[\[91a.5\]]gos so/_/sems can kun la phan don du/_/sangs rgyas kun la sbyor ba yis/_/gzhan gyi nor rnams phrog na yang /_/de la sdig pas mi gos so/_/'dod chags lta bu'i bde ba med/_/de ni rgyal ba rnams la phul/_/sems can don du gzhan bud med/_/bsten
[\[91a.6\]]pas bsod nams thob par 'gyur/_/sems can kun la phan don du/_/sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyu yi phyir/_/mi dge bcu sogs spyad pa yang /_/bsod nams rnam mang 'phel zhes gsungs/_par 'jug pa nas bzung ba/_/pha dang ma ni gsad par bya/_/rgyal
[\[91a.7\]]po ngan pa bkur mi bya/_/bram ze'i grong khyer gzhom par bya/_/des kyang grong bar gsungs pa ste/_/dgos pa bshad pa zhes ni bya/_/drang ba'i don ni theg pa gsum dang dgu ru bstan pa'o/_/yod pas nyan thos rang rgyal rnams ni smos/_/phra rab rdzas su 'dod pa nyan thos
[\[91b\]]
[\[91b.1\]]rnams/_/byang chub sems dpa' de ni byis pa'i rang bzhin no/_/med par zhen cing chags par 'dod pa'i byis pa ste/_/theg pa dman pa log pa'i shes pa ste/_/de kho de la de yi theg bstan pa/_/zhes rgyud las gsungs so/_/yang dag don dang ldan gyur pa/_/stong
[\[91b.2\]]nyid rang bzhin lhug pa ni/_/byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dngos/_/blang dor med pa thar pa'i lam/_/lung las kyang /_byang chub sems dpa' chen po sbyin pa ni bcing ba'o/_/tshul khrims nas ye shes kyi bar du ni bcing ba'o/_/bde ba dang /_stong pa dang /_rig pa dang /_bdag
[\[91b.3\]]med pa ni bcing ba'o/_/ci'i phyir zhe na bdag thams cad dang bral ba'i phyir ro/_/de nas bral ba'i chos la yang rigs kyi bu'am/_rigs kyi bu mo bslab par mi bya'o/_/des na mu stegs pa la sogs pa'i bdag lta dang /_byis pa rnams kyi yod pa'i shes pa rnams ni gzhom
[\[91b.4\]]pa sla'o/_/bdag med dang /_rig stong la sogs pa phyogs bral gyi bdag rnams ni gzhom par dka' ba yin pa'i phyir 'khor ba las mi thar ba bstan to/_/des na 'dod pa lam du byas pa'i bcing ba'o/_/bya ba med pa thob pa med pa ni nges pa'i don zhes bya'o/_/de skad gsungs pa
[\[91b.5\]]yin pa'i phyir/_/de ni dus phun sum tshogs pa'o/_/gnod sbyin thams cad yongs su rgyu/_/shin tu dben pa shin tu yongs dag pa/_/zhes pas gnas phun sum tshogs pa bstan pa yin te/_gnod sbyin thams cad yongs su rgyu ba ni ri rab rtse mo ste/_de na ni gnod sbyin gang ba bzang po dang /_
[\[91b.6\]]nor bu bzang po dang lngas rtsen la sogs pa ste/_gnod sbyin gos sngon can gyi 'khor du bstan te/_de na ni gnod sbyin ma rungs pa gzhan yang yod pa ste/_de rnams yod pa ni gnod sbyin thams cad yongs su rgyu ba zhes bya'o/_/shin tu dben pa ni stug po bkod pa'i gnas te/_'di
[\[91b.7\]]yang dpe shel gsal ba'i nang du chud pa'i dkyil 'khor gsal ba ni/_gzhal yas khang 'dug pa ni ma lus pa'i lhun gyis grub pa'i rgyan dang ldan zhes bya'o/_/de na ye shes chen po ston pa bzhugs te/_'khor dang chos la sogs pa gcig tu bzhugs te me dang tsha ba
[\[92a\]]
[\[92a.1\]]bzhin no/_/rang bzhin gcig par shes par bya'o/_/des na gnas gsum mo/_/gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can zhes bya ba/_dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis las kyi khro bo'i dbang bskur ba zhes bya bar
