[\[92a.3\]]sbyin rnams ston pa'i gzi brjid kyis/_nye ba'i 'khor byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis sprul pa'i sbrul gyi rgyan btab ces bya bar bstan to/_/stag gi sham thabs dang gos sngon po bla gos rnams ni/_gnod sbyin bred pa'i stobs kyis skyabs kyi 'od la phul zhes bya'o/_/dus
[\[92a.4\]]gsum bde gshegs zhes bya ba ni/_byang chub sems dpa' phyag na rdo rje bcu la gnas pa'i tshe/_pad+ma stong dang ldan pa'i dbus su bzhag ste/_dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi thugs kyi stong pa nyid kyi rdo rje phyung nas phyag na rdo rje thugs kyi bdag por sdud pa por dbang bskur
[\[92a.5\]]zhing bka' gnang nas/_las thams cad bting phan chad kyis zhes pa'o/_/mche ba gtsigs pa/_yid khros pa lta bu/_mig me mdag gi phung po 'dra ba/_dbugs me ltar 'bar ba/_'jigs pa'i nga ro can zhes pa la mche ba gtsigs pas ni log par rtog pa'i bdud
[\[92a.6\]]rnams za zhing 'joms pa'o/_/yid khros pas ni don snying rje chen po dang ldan pa yin te/_kun rdzob tu khro bo'i cha byad do/_/mig me mdag gi phung po ni/_las gnyis la 'jug_/rang smin pa'i las dang bltas pa tsam gyis 'jigs par byed pa'o/_/dbugs me lce ltar
[\[92a.7\]]'bar ba ni/_smin ma dang sgra tsam gyis 'dul bar bstan to/_/'jigs pa'i nga ro ni ngag gi skyon bzhi dang bral zhing yid kyi zug rngu 'don zhing /_hUM dang phaT kyi sgra sgrogs pas 'khor rnams skrag pa'o/_/lag pa dang rkang pa klu nor rgyas kyis brgyan pa/_klu nag po se ral
[\[92b\]]
[\[92b.1\]]khar thogs pa/_klu nag po dang nye dga' bos snyan cha brgyan pa zhes pa ni/_lag pa la sbrul nag po dang ser pos brgyan par shes par bya'o/_/rkang pa la sbrul nag pos brgyan pa'i ska rags dmar po byas pa'o/_/se ral kha ni kla khengs po'i rigs kyis ga shar byas pa'o/_/
[\[92b.2\]]klu dga' bo dang nye dga' bo'i ming yin la/_de dang 'dra ba'i sbrul dkar pos snyan cha brgyan par bstan to/_/sbrul 'bar ba rin po che'i cod pan thogs pa/_sbrul gdug pa 'bar ba za zhes pa la/_sbrul 'bar ba rin po che'i cod pan thogs pa ni/_dbu la nor bu rin po
[\[92b.3\]]ches brgyan pa'o/_/'bar ba ni nag po la sogs pa'i kha dog bzhin/_sbrul rin po che dang ldan pas dbu la brgyan par bstan to/_/gdug pa za ba ni zhal du sbrul nag po gsol bar bstan to/_/des kyang gtso bo 'dod chags rnam par dag pa dang /_tshul khrims nyams
[\[92b.4\]]pa'i skyon dang bral zhing /_phyi rol gyi klu'i rigs drug 'dul ba'i rtags su bstan/_/bzhin rgyas pa/_smin ma dpral bar bsdus pa/_ya sos ma mchu mnan pa/_gshin rje'i cha byad can zhes bya ba ni/_bzhin rgyas pa ni stong pa nyid kyi don rgyas pas gdong gi 'phel
[\[92b.5\]]ba ste/_lha la sogs pa gdul bya 'dul bar bstan to/_/ya sos ma mchu mnan pa ni/_ya sos ma mchu'i steng du phyin pa ste/_bye brag tu srin po 'dul ba'i rtags so/_/smin ma dpral bar bsdus pa ni/_khro gnyer gsum dpral bar 'dug pa sku gsum dang ldan
[\[92b.6\]]pa'i rtags/_gshin rje'i cha byad can ni khro bo mi'u thung gi gzugs 'dra ba'o/_/des ni gshin rje'i rigs 'dul ba'o/_/lce glog ltar 'gyu ba/_sbrul za ba/_gsus pa che ba/_lag pa brdabs pa'i sgras 'jigs par byed pa zhes bya ba ni/_lce glog ltar 'gyu ba ni/_sprul pa glog
[\[92b.7\]]pas myur ba'o/_/sbrul za ba ni sbrul klu'i nad ngan 'dra bas 'dod chags kyi gdung ba sel ba'o/_/gsus pa che ba ni gsus khyim che ba ste/_stong pa nyid kyang bstan to/_/lag pa brdabs pa ni gtso bo lag pa rdo rje dang ldan pas ma rungs pa 'jigs par byed pa'o/_/klu'i rgyal
[\[93a\]]
[\[93a.1\]]po 'dab bzangs ska rags su bcings pa/_a la la zhes sgrogs par byed pa zhes pa la/_'dab bzangs ni sbrul dmar po'i ska rags su bcings pa/_a la la ni de 'dra'i rgyan cha la ngo mtshar ba'o/_/de sgrogs pa ni sgra sgrogs pa'o/_/rgya mtsho'i zabs su
[\[93a.2\]]dpag tshad brgyad khri bzhi stong yod pa rkang pa'i pus mor phyin pa/_dbang po dang nyi ma phrag pa la khur zhes pa la/_rgya mtsho la dpag tshad brgyad khri yod pas phyag na rdo rje'i bus mo nub pa/_sku byin po la nyis 'bum drug khri yod pa zhes pa ste/_sprul pa'i sku'i bong tshad bstan to/_/dbang
[\[93a.3\]]po dang nyi ma ni thabs shes rab kyi ste/_nang gtso bo bzhugs zhes pa la/_yang na gtso bo'i phrag pa la nyi zla rgyu ba ste zhes pa'i tshad do/_/la la na re lha'i dbang po'i phrag pa la nyi zla rgyu ste/_de'i steng na phyag na rdo rje bzhugs zhes pa ste/_lha 'dul ba'o/_/klu thams cad rlag par
[\[93a.4\]]byed pa/_gad rgyangs chen po dgod pas kun du 'khrugs par byed pa zhes pa la/_klu'i rigs kyi bdag po la sogs pa brlag pa'i phyir/_ha ha zhes bya ba'i sgra drangs pa'i phyir ro/_/gad rgyangs ni ha sa de ba ta'i sgra bsgrags pas klu thams cad sngangs shing brgyal te sha rus khro bo'i
[\[93a.5\]]zhal du stobs zhes pa'o/_/klu thams cad 'ching bar byed pa/_'byung po thams cad 'gugs shing zhi bar mdzad pa zhes bya ba la/_'byung po'i bdag po dbang ldan la sogs pa 'gugs shing bcing ba ste/_lcags kyu'i sbyor bas bkug nas/_dkar gsum dang mngar
[\[93a.6\]]gsum dang ldan pa'i gtor ma sbyin zhes pa'o/_/klu thams cad ces pa ni/_bcing ba ni gcod mi nus te/_gzhan gshin rje dang 'byung po spyi yang yongs su bzung ba ste/_sbyor ba thams cad gcod par mdzad pa/_sbyor ba thams cad zlog par mdzad pa/_sbyor ba thams cad gnon par
[\[93a.7\]]mdzad pa/_yon tan ma lus pa'i bdag po de zhes pa la sbyor ba ni phyi'i drug dang /_khrag dang sngags kyis byas pa'i gnod pa ste/_gzhan gyis byas pa'i rig sngags tshur mi tshugs par bzlog pa'o/_/sbyor ba bzlog pa ni rang bsrung ba dang pha rol rang la bzlog pa'o/_/sbyor ba gnon pa ni pha rol
[\[93b\]]
[\[93b.1\]]bzlog pa'i 'khor lo thod pa mi mthun pas gnon zhes pa'o/_/tshig de gsum yang zab pa'i phyir bla ma'i man ngag la rag las par bya ba'i phyir bshad par mi bya'o/_/yon tan ni sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad dang /_stobs bcu dang mi 'jigs pa bzhi dang /_so so
[\[93b.2\]]yang dag par rig pa bzhi dang /_byams pa la sogs pa'i yon tan dang ldan pa'o/_/des kyang gnas khyad par can na ston pa yon tan dang ldan pa bzhugs par bstan to/_/gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon nyi shu rtsa brgyad dang /_gnod sbyin mthu bo che thams cad ces pas 'khor
[\[93b.3\]]phun sum tshogs par bstan te/_rang gi 'khor ni sa bcu'i byang chub sems dpa' lag na rdo rje dang lha dang mi dang mi ma yin pa la sogs pa'o/_/gzhan yang rigs lnga'i khro bo dang lha mo dang /_sgo ma la sogs pa'i nang nas khro bo khams gsum rnam rgyal langs te/_'di
[\[93b.4\]]skad gsol zhes 'og dang 'brel to/_/bar du gcod pa'i phyir gnod sbyin smos te gang ba bzang po dang /_nor bu bzang po dang /_ldas rtsen la sogs pa nyi shu rtsa brgyad do/_/gnod sbyin mthu bo che thams cad dang zhes pa la mthu ni rang gi 'khor rnams thams cad la 'dul sems
[\[93b.5\]]can thams cad la shing gi yol gos chu 'thor ba'o/_/gnod sbyin drag po thams cad ni sha rlon pa rjen par tha ba'o/_/de ni lha min dang lha dang gnod sbyin ma rungs pa 'dul ba yang shes par bya'o/_/lha thams cad dang /_klu thams cad dang /_dri za thams cad dang /_lha ma yin
[\[93b.6\]]thams cad dang zhes pa lha ni brgyad de/_lha dang /_lha'i dbang po dang /_lha min bdag_/ma hA de ba dang /_khyab 'jug chen po dang /_u ma de ba/_kun du rgyug_/'chi med dbang po'o/_/klu yang dga' bo la sogs pa brgyad de/_de yang 'khor dang bcas pa'o/_/dri za
[\[93b.7\]]ni zur phud lnga pa'o/_/lha ma yin ni thags bzangs ris 'khor dang bcas pa'o/_/nam mkha' lding thams cad dang /_mi'am ci thams cad dang /_lto 'phye chen po thams cad dang /_'byung po dang zhes pa la/_nam mkha' lding ni gser mig can 'khor dang bcas
[\[94a\]]
[\[94a.1\]]pa'o/_/mi'am ci ni ljon pa rta mgo can la sogs pa ri rab kyi khong gseng na gnas pa'o/_/lto 'phye ni lto 'phye nyid de/_mi'i lus po la sbrul gyi mgo bo la sogs pa'o/_/'byung po ni dbang ldan la sogs pa brgyad do/_/yi dgas dang brjed byed la
[\[94a.2\]]sogs pa dang thabs cig tu bzhugs te zhes bya ba la/_yi dgas ni kha nas me 'bar la sogs pa'o/_/brjed byed ni byol song gi rgyal po ri rab la gnas pa rnams so/_/thabs cig ni bskor ba'o/_/'di ltar nyi ma dang zla ba dang skar ma'i tshogs lta bu bzhugs so zhes pa la nyi zla dang 'dra ba ni
[\[94a.3\]]bden pa gnyis dang thabs shes rab dang lam gnyis la sogs pa'o/_/skar ma dang 'dra ba ni lam de dag gi yan lag gi tshogs dang thabs cig tu skar ma lta bu bzhugs zhes pa ste/_gnas der ston pa de 'khor rnams dang lhan cig tu chos gsung ngo zhes bstan/_de ni chos phun sum tshogs pa yang yongs su
[\[94a.4\]]bstan to/_/de'i chos yang zhes pa mi snang bar gyur gyi bar la dngos su bstan/_ston pa dang chos kyi byin rlabs yin pa'i phyir de ma gsungs so/_/de nas 'phags pa lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can la 'khor thams cad kyis gsol ba zhes pa la/_de nas ni
[\[94a.5\]]chos de lta bu la ston pa bzhugs te zhes pa'o/_/'phags pa ni sgrib pa rnam pa gnyis spangs pa'o/_/gong ma dang khyad par gyi don de ni sprul sku lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can no/_/de la 'khor thams cad kyi nang nas khams gsum rnam par rgyal ba langs nas bla gos
[\[94a.6\]]sngon po gsol te/_/gos sngon po can khyod ci zhes te/_khyod kyi bya ba'i las dang ngo bo ji lta bu lags/_bde gshegs kun gyi sprul pa yin nam/_sangs rgyas kun gyi sprul pa'i ngo bo khyod yin nam/_gal te sku gsung thugs kyi bdag por bsdus pa yin
[\[94a.7\]]nam/_phrin las thams cad kyi bdag por dbang bskur ba yin nam/_bdag khams gsum rnam par rgyal ba dang 'khor rnams kyis bya ba/_las bskyed rdzogs grogs dang las kyi tshogs la sogs pa ston pa'i bstan pa sangs rgyas thams cad
[\[94b\]]
[\[94b.1\]]gcig gi ngo bo las kyi bya rgyud ji lta bu lags/_bdag cag gis bka' nyan gyi khyod kyi sku gsung thugs drag por bstan pa ni/_lam nye ba ste 'khor ba las myur du sgrol zhal pa'o/_/de bdag cag 'khor dang bcas pa rnams ston pas gsungs pa nyan to zhes pa'i
[\[94b.2\]]don to/_/le'u gang la ming de yod pa la de skad ces bya ste/_gleng gzhi phun sum tshogs pa lnga yod pas/_de la dang po gleng gzhi'i le'u zhes bya'o/_/lag ni rdo rje rtsa ba'i rgyud las gleng gzhi'i le'u ste le'u dang po'i bshad pa'o//_//de ltar
[\[94b.3\]]gleng gzhi bstan kyang bskyed rdzogs kyi don ma bstan na 'grub par mi 'gyur bas da ni le'u gnyis pa bstan to/_/des na lag na rdo rjes rdo rjes rdo rje drag po zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/_'di skad gsungs so zhes pa la/_de nas zhes bya ba
[\[94b.4\]]la/_de nas kyi sgra ni gleng gzhi song ba'i rting de nas/_bar cis kyang ma chod par lag na rdo rje'i ston pa sku gsung thugs drag po'i chos gsum gyi ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par bzhugs te 'di skad gsungs zhes bya bar sbyar ro/_/phyag rgya gsang sngags thugs
[\[94b.5\]]sbyor la/_/khro bo'i rgyal po bsam par bya/_/khro bo rdo rje'i ting 'dzin gyi/_/byin rlabs ya mtshan sna tshogs ldan/_/zhes bya ba la/_bla ma gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa'i rim pa/_phyag rgya ni srung ba dang bsod nams kyi tshogs dang ye shes dngos sam
[\[94b.6\]]gzhal yas khang bskyed pa la sogs pa'o/_/gsang sngags ni gzhal yas khang gi nang du seng ge dang pad+ma la sogs pa'i steng du/_snying rje'i stobs kyis ngo bo hUM du byung ba'o/_/thugs sbyar ni yig 'bru las phyag mtshan du gyur pa ste/_las gnyis byas pa'o/_/de

[\[95b.1\]]nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra hUM/_oM bud+d+ha kro d+ha nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra hUM/_oM rat+na kro d+ha nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra hUM/_oM pad+ma kro d+ha nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra hUM/_oM karma kro d+ha nI lAM par d+ha ra hUM/_oM trai lokya bi dza ye hUM/_oM ma hA kA la ro Sha Na hUM/_oM bi rU T+ha ka ye hUM/_oM bai shra ba Na ye hUM/_oM badzra lA s+ye hUM/_oM badzra

[\[98b.1\]]bstan te sreg par byed pa rtsa ba'i sngags dang /_da ha da ha pa tsa zhes gsungs so/_/thogs med las rnams 'grub pa ni/_/lha'i nga rgyal dang ldan pas sngags bzlas na/_gang la bya ba 'grub ste/_dper na gnam las lce 'bab pa bzhin no/_/gnyis kyi 'og ma gsum
[\[98b.2\]]par brgyan/_/de la gnyis kyi gong ldan pas/_/zung rab zung ming dang ldan pa/_/yang ming skul dang bsam gtan ni/_/lcags kyu sbyor bas rab tu bya/_/zhes pa la/_gnyis kyi 'og ma ni shes rab kyi yi ge gnyis pa'o/_/gsum pa thabs kyi yi ge ring por gsum pa'o/_/

[\[103a.1\]]pa'i rdzu 'phrul can/_/bu smad bcas shing g.yog 'khor bcas pa rnams/_/gnas nas phan gdags phyir ni 'dir gshegs shig_/srid pa'i rtse nas dmyal ba'i gnas yan chad/_/rgyud drug skye 'gro ma lus thams cad kun/_/gnas nas phan

[\[135a.1\]]'ba' zhig pa dang bcas pa dang /_phra mo'i ting nge 'dzin dang bcas pa dang /_mgal me lta bu dang phreng ba nyi ma lta bu'i rigs bdag gi mtshan mngon du byed do/_/las khyad par gyi dus su yang so so'i bsam gtan dang bcas pa las grub par byed pa'o/_/

[\[158a.4\]]yi ge gsum las legs grub pa'i/_/sku gsum lha ru gsal ba la/_/ye shes spyan drangs mchod nas bstims/_/gnyis med 'gyur la mchod phul te/_/'od dang sngags kyis bskul gyur te/_/'od zhu byang chub thig le'am/_/yang na 'od kyi gong bur gyur/_/byang chub tshon

[\[180b.1\]]chen lam la rab gnas nas/_/gos sngon dngos grub thob par shog_/gtor ma'i rgyan gyi man ngag dge slong klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//[ {D2209}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_sa ma yA laM kA ra/_bod skad du/_dam tshig gi rgyan/_phyag na rdo rje la phyag
[\[180b.2\]]'tshal lo/_/dam tshig med dang 'chal par gtong /_/som nyi la sogs bsal ba'i phyir/_/dam tshig rnams ni mdor bsdus nas/_/gsang ba'i bdag la 'dud de bshad/_/sngags pas srung ba'i dam tshig ni/_/dang po byang chub sems bskyed nas/_/nya 'am stong gi dus
[\[180b.3\]]dag tu/_/yan lag brgyad pa nyer gnas te/_/lo gcig pa'am zla gcig bya/_/de nas ji srid sems bskyed de/_/bslab pa lnga po legs bzung nas/_/lo gcig zla gcig bar dag tu/_/sdom pa brtan por gzung bar bya/_/de nas dge tshul dge slong gi/_/bslab pa la ni
[\[180b.4\]]legs gnas te/_/mi gtong lo 'am zla ba 'am/_/sdom pa nyams pa blang bar bya/_/so sor thar pa'i sdom pa la/_/gang zhig gis ni legs gnas na/_/mkhas pa rnams kyis dus kun du/_/srog gi phyir yang mi gtong ngo /_/gang zhig gis ni de goms 'gyur/_/gang tshe gong
[\[180b.5\]]ma'i bslab gnas pas/_/de tshe 'og ma'i ming dang bral/_/dang po sbyin pa bslab bya ste/_/dngos po bcu gnyis yang dag ldan/_/bzod dang brtson 'grus bsam gtan dang /_/shes rab gsum ste gsum du bstan/_/gzhan gyi mya ngan sangs la sogs/_/sems can don 'gyur
[\[180b.6\]]thams cad kun/_/srog gi phyir yang mi gtong ngo /_/sdom pa lo 'am zla ba ru/_/brtan nas sngags kyi dam tshig blang /_/spyi dang khyad par gnyis su shes/_/dang po dag ni bshad bya ste/_/dang por slob dpon mnyes par bya/_/yi dam spong len mi bya ste/_/lus dang ngag yid sku gsung

[\[181a.1\]]mi bya/_/khyad par grogs la smos ci dgos/_/tshogs dang gtor ma sbyin sreg bya/_/maN+Dal tsha tsha la sogs pa/_/srog gi phyir yang mi gtong ngo /_/chos kyi spyod pa gzhan rnams kyang /_/spang bar 'gyur ba smos ci dgos/_/sha chen khrag

[\[189b.3\]]tshig blang /_/zhes pa la/_sdom pa de rnams rim pas len pa ni gang zag spros bcas la dga' ba'i don du gsungs pa'o/_/theg pa chen po'i rigs can la ni/_sdom pa gsum gdan thog tu blang /_/zhes pa'o/_/sngags kyi dam tshig blang ba ni/_/bla ma sdom pa gsum dang ldan pa las dbang
[\[189b.4\]]blang zhing /_dbang bzhi dang 'brel pa'i dam tshig gsum pa'o/_/spyi dang khyad par gnyis su shes ni/_spyi gsang sngags phyi nang gi dam tshig dang /_khyad par gsang ba'i bdag po'i dam tshig go/_/dang po dag ni bshad bya ni/_sngags spyi'i dam tshig go/_/dang po slob dpon mnyes
[\[189b.5\]]par bya/_/yi dam spang len mi bya ste/_/lus ngag yid gsum sku gsung thugs/_/phyag rgya che la rab tu gnas/_/zhes pa la/_dang po dbang gi dus su bla ma yo byad dang spyod pas mnyes par bya ba'o/_/dbang thob par bya ste/_phyis de bzhin du bla ma dang dam pa rnams la/_rang gis lus
[\[189b.6\]]ngag yid kyi nyes pa med cing mos par bya/_zhes pa dang nyes pa che chung gi tshogs dang /_gtor ma brgyad dang 'bum la sogs pas bshags pa bya'o/_/yi dam spong len mi bya ni/_/shes pas gong ma'i lha spangs na/_/rtsa ba chad de ngan song 'gro/_/zhes pa ni de ni mnar med pa'o/_/
[\[189b.7\]]shul gyi don la lha snga ma'i 'bras bu yod pa bstims te gnyis med byas na'am/_/gnyis snang med par gcig gi ngo bo byung na ma spangs pa'o/_/lus ngag yid phyag rgya chen po ni/_/lus lha dang ngag gi rdo rje'i bzlas pa dang /_sems phyag rgya chen po dang mi 'brel pa ste mi dge

[\[190a.1\]]ba bcu med pa ni phyag rgya chen po la rab tu gnas zhes bya'o/_/dam pa rnams ni smad mi bya/_/gsang ba'i don yang bstan mi bya/_/rtags chen sku yang mi bstan te/_/bzlas dang sems nyams bstan mi bya/_/zhes pa la/_dam pa rnams ni bla ma dam pa'am sangs
[\[190a.2\]]rgyas 'byung ba'i bla ma dam pa ste/_de la smad na sangs rgyas la mnyes pa mi bgyis pa ste/_chos med pa'i yul du skye zhes pa'o/_/gsang ba'i don ni gsang sngags kyi don dang /_dbang gnyis pa gsum pa'i man ngag rnams dang /_rdo rje'i spun ma yin pa la mi bstan pa ste/_bstan na
[\[190a.3\]]sngags kyi dngos grub yal/_/zhes pa'o/_/rtags chen su yang mi bstan te/_/rang gi ltag pa'i sku'i rtags rnams phyi pa la mi bstan te/_bstan na lhag pa'i lha'i dngos grub mi 'byung ba'o/_/bzlas na sems nyams mi bstan na/_/rang gi rdo rje spun min pa la bzlas pa'i spyod pa dang /_

[\[190b.1\]]'grogs pa'i phyir grogs so/_/bsrung ba'i phyir bsrung ba'o/_/tshogs dang gtor ma sbyin sreg dang /_/maN+Dal tsha tsha la sogs pa/_/srog gi phyir yang mi gtong ngo /_/tshogs dang gtor ma dang tsha tsha la sogs pa rnams/_lus la me 'bar bas myur bar bya ste/_dus rkyen

[\[191a.1\]]che'i rigs kyi gang zag rnams la mi smad ces pa'o/_/ye shes ngos 'dzin med par de spang ba'ang min blang ba'ang min/_gang zag gnyis kyis so/_/bgrod min la ni bgrod pa min/_/spang ba mi spong 'gyur ba dang /_/blang bya mi len spang bar bya/_/zhes pa la/_theg pa

[\[192a.1\]]bas mchod cing dang ba dang mos pas mnyes par bya ste/_'jig rten pa'i lha la mi mchod ces so/_/rtag tu bla ma mnyes pa ni/_/dbang gi dus su yon gyis bla ma mnyes pa las dbang thob par bya ste/_phyis bla ma dang ma nyams par dam pa'i chos dang mthun pas bla ma

[\[240a.4\]]mchod pa nyid do/_/'di'i mchod pas kyang yid du 'ong ba'i rdzas phun sum tshogs pa dang phun sum tshogs pa la sogs te/_bsod nams dam pa 'thob par 'gyur ro/_/mchod pa'i tshogs bshad zin to/_/da ni bdud brtag pa'i sbyor ba bshad par bya ste/_dang po bdud
[\[240a.5\]]'byung ba'i dus ni/_sngags dang bsam gtan dus dag tu/_/zhes pa ste/_sgrub pa'i skabs yin pa'i phyir gzhan du ni nyan pa dang bsam pa las 'byung bar 'gyur ro/_/bdud kyang du zhig ce na/_phyi dang nang na yod pa'o/_/zhes pa ji skad bshad pa dang de las gzhan pa'i bdud

[\[240a.7\]]pa'i rtags dang bye brag med do zhe na/_gsal ba'i 'od ni sangs rgyas te/_/zhes pa dngos po la gsal bar gyur pa ni sangs rgyas kyi 'od de/_de las bzlog pa ni bzlog pa'o zhe'o/_/'di yang dngos po la yin te/_shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa las lha rnams kyi 'od
[\[240b\]]
[\[240b.1\]]mog mog por gyur pa la sogs pa brjod pa bzhin no/_/sgra'i bdud bye brag tu bstan pa ni/_rang bzhin med dris dman pa dang /_/zhes pa ni/_de kho na nyid ji lta ba bzhin du ston par mi nus pa'o/_/spyod pa ni mtshan ma las spyod pa ste de'i rigs ma yin pa la de gtsor ston pa

[\[240b.3\]]gzhan go sla/_nang gi bdud kyi sbyor ba ni gnyis te zhes khong nas dbyung ngo /_/gang yin zhe na/_'du ba skye dang bsam pa sgyur/_/zhes pa chos 'di gnyis kyi ting nge 'dzin las g.yengs te/_dngos grub kyi bar du gcod pa nyid do/_/dang po bshad pa/_rlung mkhris bad kan 'dus

[\[241a\]]
[\[241a.1\]]su 'phro ba ste/_snga ma bzhin du gnas pa'o/_/bsam gtan 'phro la dmigs pa gsal ba ni glo bur du bying ba'o/_/nyams mi dga' ba ni sems reg par mi gnas pa'o/_/log pa la dang ba ni mu stegs dang sngags rgod dang bud med sbyor sngags la dad

[\[241b.1\]]mtshan ma'o/_/dam tshig rnams ni mi brjed cing /_/zhes pa ni rmi lam du yang dam tshig rjes su dran pa'o/_/rang gi rigs kyi bu mo bsten/_/zhes pa ni/_rang dang 'phrod pa'i phyag rgya ma dang mthun par gnas pa'o/_/gzhan go sla/_gzhan gyis mchod pa ni rang la'o/_/

[\[242a\]]
[\[242a.1\]]zhes pa ni rang dang tha dad du mi rtog pa'o/_/nga rgyal la sogs nyon mongs chung /_/zhes pa ni snga ma las shes chung du gyur pa'o/_/zab pa'i don la chog mi shes/_/zhes pa ni chog par mi 'dzin pa'o/_/gzhan ni sbyin pa'i bye brag go/_/ldang ba yang ba nyid zo mdog bde ba

[\[242b.1\]]gnyis pa'i dus su'o/_/'gul ba dang 'phar ba ni dang po'i dus su'o/_/dkar dmar la sogs zhes pa ni gang gis ser po dang ljang gu la yang ste/_gsal ba dang mi gsal ba yang sangs rgyas kyi rtags yin no/_/gang gi sgo na sbyin zhe na/_sgyu ma tsam du

[\[243a.1\]]ni sgyu ma lta bu'o/_/chos thams cad ni ye nas don dam par gang yang ma grub pa'o zhes bya bar nges pa de'i rjes su thob pa rnams kyi'o/_/log pa'i rtags kyang thob la 'bras bu med pa'ang yod de/_dga' ba dang skrag pa'i sems dang ldan

[\[243a.6\]]dang /_/byang chub sems la spyod byed pa/_/zhes pa ni/_brtul zhugs kyi spyod pas bdud rtsi lnga la spyod pas bzlog par 'gyur ba'i phyir ro/_/gang gis dam tshig rtag tu srung /_/de la bdud kyi sbyor ba med/_/ces pa ni/_gang gis sdom pa phun sum
[\[243a.7\]]tshogs par gyur na bdud thams cad nye bar zhi bar 'gyur ro/_/yi dam lha la lus 'bul zhing /_/dam tshig nyams pa bshags pa dang /_/phyis ni sdom pa 'dzin byed pa/_/zhes pa ni/_gang gi tshe rang gi yi dam gyi lha la lus phul ba la sogs pas

[\[243b.1\]]de'i gnod pa zhi bar 'gyur ro/_/de la drag po'i sbyor sngags dang /_/mi 'da' gsang ba'i sngags zlos zhes pa ni/_dam tshig gi sngags dang /_drag po chen po khro bo'i sngags kyis bzlog pa'o/_/bdag las byung ba'i zhes pa rang las khro bo gdug

[\[243b.3\]]sla'o/_/yang na bdag nyid khro bo yi/_/mdun gyi snying du sems dpa' bskyed/_/zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i don ni gang gis thog ma nyid du sems dpa' snying ga nas phyung ste/_de'i snying du bcug nas nges pa'i mtshan ma ston cig ces las bcol te/_khro bo

[\[243b.6\]]rdo rje gos sngon po'i rnal 'byor gyis ni rdo rje sdigs mdzub bo/_/las kyi gos sngon can gyi rnal 'byor gyis ni rgya gram mo/_/bde gshegs gos sngon po can gyi rnal 'byor gyis ni 'khor lo'i phyag rgya'o/_/bkra shis 'khor lo'i sbyor ba yis/_/zhes pa ni gnyen po'i ting nge 'dzin gyis so/_/ji ltar

[\[244a\]]
[\[244a.1\]]dga' ba bsgom pa'o/_/gti mug la sogs chos rnams dbye/_/zhes pa ni dge ba dang mi dge ba la sogs pas dbye'o/_/gzhan go sla'o/_/gal te brda dang phyag rgya la sogs pa'i sbyor ba ston gyur na zhes pa ni/_brda dang phyag rgya dang gar dang glu la sogs pa ston pa'o/_/

[\[244a.4\]]sogs pas bzlog par bya'o/_/bskyed pa'i rim pa la gnas pa'i bdud la ni/_gang gi mtshan ma'i ting nge 'dzin ji skad smos pas zhi bar bya'o/_/rdzogs pa'i rim pa'i ting nge 'dzin la gnas pas ni stong pa nyid la sogs pas zhi bar bya'o/_/yang na sngags zlos pa ni bskyed pa'i ting nge 'dzin
[\[244a.5\]]la sogs pa'o/_/bskyed pa'i ting nge 'dzin la sgyu ma lta bus so/_/gang gi tshe rdzogs pa'i ting nge 'dzin la bskyed pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyis shes na ni nyes pa dang bcas shing 'gal ba dang bcas par 'gyur ro/_/bdud bzlog pa'i cho ga bshad zin to/_/de ltar spyod pa'i rim pa bstan zin to/_/
[\[244a.6\]]da ni thun mong gi dngos grub bstan par bya ste/_de la dang po 'byung po tshar gcad pa'i cho ga bstan pa'i phyir/_gang zhig bdag dang gzhan rnams la/_/zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te/_de las gzhi yid 'ong zhes pa ni bshad zin to/_/sngon du 'gro ba rdzogs pa dang /_/zhes pa ni/_sa'i
[\[244a.7\]]cho ga la sogs pa rdzogs pa'o/_/gang ltar 'dod pa'i sku bskyed de/_/zhes pa ni dbang thob par byas pa las byung ba'i sku g.yon na phyogs skyong gi rgyal po gang yang rung ba thogs pa bskyed pa'o/_/zhi ba la sogs so so yi/_/bzlas dang bsdu ba rdzogs gyur nas/_/zhes pa ni/_rang dang
[\[244b\]]
[\[244b.1\]]ba'i sku mdun du bltas te/_de la mchod pa dang bstod pa byas nas gang yin pa'i ming dang las kyi sngags spel te/_grangs brgya'am stong du rdzogs pa dang /_'khor lo rang la bsdus te/_zhi bar gyur pa'i tshogs dag dang /_/gtor mas kyang ni bzlog par bya/_/zhes pa thog ma nyid du zhi
[\[244b.2\]]ba'i tshogs dang gtor mas bzlog pa'o/_/de yis 'dul bar ma gyur na/_/zhes pa ni des ma zhi na stang stabs kyis gdul zhe'o/_/de nyid bshad pa/_rkang pa ral gri g.yas pa la/_/zhes pa ni rkang pa g.yas pa ral gri rab tu 'bar ba sbrul dang chu srin la sogs pas mdzes par byas
[\[244b.3\]]pa bsam mo/_/g.yon pa lcags kyu'i sbyor ba zhes pa rkang pa g.yon pa lcags kyu rab tu 'bar ba 'od sna tshogs dang ldan par bsam mo/_/des ci bya zhe na/_mi g.yo g.yas g.yon stang stabs bya/_/zhes pa mi 'gyur ba tha mal pa'i 'gros kyi tshul la cung zad bteg nas dgug pa
[\[244b.4\]]dang gdab pa'i tshul bya'o/_/sngags 'og nas ston to/_/las gzhan bstan pa/_nad pa'am ni gzugs dag la/_/dmigs pa len par dbab bya ste/_/zhes pa ni 'byung po nad pa'am gzugs la bsdu'o zhes pa'i don to/_/rkang pa g.yas pa ri rab ni/_/rgya gram

[\[249a.6\]]thig ler 'dod/_/ces pa ni/_thig le dkar dmar gyis dbab pa ni/_bde ba'i rgyan no/_/a thung dun gyis dbab pa ni/_a wa d+hU tI pa'o/_/bzhi ni so sor slob pa ste/_/zhes pa ni gong du bshad pa nyid do/_/gcig ni mdud par slob pa'o/_/zhes pa ni 'og nas ston
[\[249a.7\]]to/_/gzhan go sla/_gang gis rdo rje'i sbyor ba yis/_/zhes pa ni gsang ba'i rdo rje'i 'khor lo la slob pa'o/_/sum cu gnyis dang zhes bya ba la sogs pas ni rtse mo dang rked pa dang de'i cha dang rtsa bar bsam pa'o/_/bzhi po kho na zhes pa ni/_rtse mo la sogs par rlung
[\[249b\]]
[\[249b.1\]]gi 'gro ldog gis bsdu'o/_/brgyad ni steng 'og gnyi ga'i sbyor ba'o/_/gnyis ni bde ba chen po gnyis la ste dbab pa dang /_bzlog pa'i bye brag go/_/dbab pas dga' ba skye ba dang /_/zhes pa la sogs pa ni byang chub kyi sems gnas pa'i bye brag gi dbang du byas pa'o/_/da ni rnal 'byor ma la
[\[249b.2\]]brten pa'i cho ga bshad pa/_gang tshe rang gi rigs mthun pa/_/zhes pa ni/_rang la mdzes pa'i rgyan yod pa'o/_/byin gyis brlabs nas gnyis med sbyor/_/zhes pa ni/_gsang ba'i snying po byin gyis brlabs nas rdo rjer zhugs pa'o/_/des dga' ba rnams rim gyis bskyed pa'o/_/shes
[\[249b.3\]]rab ma'i dbye ba bstan pa las las skyes pa ni/_khu khrag dang bcas pa las skyes pa'i bu mo'o/_/ye shes kyi bu mo ni bde bar gshegs pa las sprul pa'o/_/g.yon gyi yum ni g.yon gyi yum nyid do/_/snying gar byung ba ni sa bon las sprul pa'i bu mo'o/_/rkang pa thi gus bcing ba ni lag pa dam
[\[249b.4\]]du 'khyud de bsdams pa'o/_/dbugs kyi lcags kyu bzlog pa ni dbugs gyen du drangs pa'o/_/gzhan go sla/_nyi ma'i me ni lte bar 'bar/_/zhes pa ni/_gang gis lte ba nas ting nge 'dzin gyis gtum mo sbar te/_sa bon bkug pa'o/_/yang na 'byed 'dzums sbyong ba yis/_/zhes bya ba la
[\[249b.5\]]sogs pa ni 'byed 'dzums kyis rlung sngon po bskyod pa la sogs pa'i bde ba chen po nas/_byang chub kyi sems bkug ste/_'khor lo rim gyis gang bar bsam pa'o/_/rnal 'byor ma zhes pa la sogs pa'i don ni/_longs spyod dang sprul pa'i gnas su sa bon bsam pa'o/_/thabs ni zhes pa la
[\[249b.6\]]sogs pa'i don ni/_bde ba chen po dang chos kyi 'khor lo sa bon gyis rgyas pa'o/_/sbrul gyi zhags pas zhes pa la sogs pa'i don no/_ting nge 'dzin la sogs pas haM las sa bon byung ba zhu nas kun du 'khyil par bsam pa'o/_/de nas 'khor lo rgyas pa'i dus bstan pa ni/_gang gis gtso bo'i
[\[249b.7\]]sbyor ba la/_/zhes pa la sogs pa ste/_gtso bo'i ting nge 'dzin gsal nas/_de las gzhan du zhu bar gyur pa'o/_/yang na rnal 'byor bde chen por/_/gsal nas khyab pa'i spu ldang zhing /_/snang ba gsum ni 'byung bar 'gyur/_/zhes bya ba ni/_gang gis haM la blo gtad de gsal ba dang /_smig rgyu la sogs
[\[250a\]]
[\[250a.1\]]pa'i rtags 'byung ba dang /[ (]sbu [,]spu [)]ldang ba dang /_'dar ba dang /_'phar ba la sogs pa byung nas haM las sa bon phab ste/_dga' ba gsum bskyed par bya'o/_/yang na 'khor lo'i sbyor spangs pas/_/zhes pa la sogs pa'i don ni/_mdud pa ni bcu drug la sogs par byang
[\[250a.2\]]chub sems kyi rim par dag pa'o/_/gang zhig 'di la rtag gnas na/_/zhes pa la sogs pa'i don ni/_dus des bskyed pa yongs su rdzogs pa la/_/'bras bu dam pa thob par 'gyur ro/_/gzhan go sla/_bdud dang gnod sbyin la sogs pa/_/zhes pa la sogs pa'i don ni/_gang zhig gis
[\[250a.3\]]thog ma nyid du byang chub tu sems bskyed pa nas bzung ba'i dge ba'i stobs kyis gnod par gyur pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pa'i phyir ro/_/da ni sgrub pa'i thabs gtad pa ni yul mi mthun pa'i phyogs dang bcas te/_bstan pa gang zhig don 'di zhes bya ba la sogs pa smos te/_/de dag gi
[\[250a.4\]]don yang kha phyir bltas pa dang nyon mongs pa mang ba dang /_ched du mi byed par gyur pa la spel na/_tshe 'di dang tshe rabs phyi ma thams cad du sdug bsngal sna tshogs nyams su myong bar 'gyur ro/_/'o na gang zhig la bstan par bya zhe na/_snod ldan zhes bya ba la sogs pa'i don ni/_gzhan la mi spel ba dang /_
[\[250a.5\]]khro ba chung ba dang /_ma chags pa dang /_mos pa dang /_dad pa dang ldan pa dang /_nga rgyal chung ba dang /_sems kyi don la dga' ba la byin na legs pa thams cad kyi rgyur 'gyur ro zhes pa'i don to/_/da ni nyes pa sbyang bar bstan pa/_bdag 'dra ma rig ces bya ba la sogs pa'i don ni shes rab zhan pa dang /_gting
[\[250a.6\]]dpag dka' bas brtsam par bya ba ma yin kyang rang bas dman pas rtogs par sla ba'i phyir bstan to zhes bya ba'i don to/_/bla na med pa'i byang chub chen por bsngo ba ni/_bdag gis bsgrubs 'di zhes pa'i don ni/_dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis bstan pa yun ring du gnas pa dang /_sems can rnams mngon par mtho ba dang /_nges par
[\[250a.7\]]legs pa thob par smon to zhes bya ba'i don to/_/de ltar bzod par gsol ba dang /_nyes pa bshags pa 'dis ni bstan bcos dman par gyur pa'i nyes bdag pa dang dge ba'i rtsa ba mi zad cing shin tu 'phel bar yang bstan to/_/de kho na nyid sgron ma'i 'grel ba slob dpon dpa' bos byin gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//_//
